a purā nāmnā hi durvāsā atreḥ putro mahāmuniḥ
c vasiṣṭhasyāśrame puṇye sa vārṣikyam uvāsa ha
a tam āśramaṃ mahātejāḥ pitā te sumahāyaśāḥ
c purodhasaṃ mahātmānaṃ didṛkṣur agamat svayam
a sa dṛṣṭvā sūryasaṃkāśaṃ jvalantam iva tejasā
c upaviṣṭaṃ vasiṣṭhasya savye pārśve mahāmunim
e tau munī tāpasa śreṣṭhau vinītas tv abhyavādayat
a sa tābhyāṃ pūjito rājā svāgatenāsanena ca
c pādyena phalamūlaiś ca so 'py āste munibhiḥ saha
a teṣāṃ tatropaviṣṭānāṃ tās tāḥ sumadhurāḥ kathāḥ
c babhūvuḥ paramarṣīṇāṃ madhyādityagate 'hani
a tataḥ kathāyāṃ kasyāṃ cit prāñjaliḥ pragraho nṛpaḥ
c uvāca taṃ mahātmānam atreḥ putraṃ tapodhanam
a bhagavan kiṃ pramāṇena mama vaṃśo bhaviṣyati
c kimāyuś ca hi me rāmaḥ putrāś cānye kimāyuṣaḥ
a rāmasya ca sutā ye syus teṣām āyuḥ kiyad bhavet
c kāmyayā bhagavan brūhi vaṃśasyāsya gatiṃ mama
a tac chrutvā vyāhṛtaṃ vākyaṃ rājño daśarathasya tu
c durvāsāḥ sumahātejā vyāhartum upacakrame
a ayodhyāyāḥ patī rāmo dīrghakālaṃ bhaviṣyati
c sukhinaś ca samṛddhāś ca bhaviṣyanty asya cānujāḥ
a kasmiṃś cit karaṇe tvāṃ ca maithilīṃ ca yaśasvinīm
c saṃtyajiṣyati dharmātmā kālena mahatā kila
a daśavarṣasahasraṇi daśavarṣaśatāni ca
c rāmo rājyam upāsitvā brahmalokaṃ gamiṣyati
a samṛddhair hayamedhaiś ca iṣṭvā parapuraṃjayaḥ
c rājavaṃśāṃś ca kākutstho bahūn saṃsthāpayiṣyati
a sa sarvam akhilaṃ rājño vaṃśasyāsya gatāgatam
c ākhyāya sumahātejās tūṣṇīm āsīn mahādyutiḥ
a tūṣṇīṃbhūte munau tasmin rājā daśarathas tadā
c abhivādya mahātmānau punar āyāt purottamam
a etad vaco mayā tatra muninā vyāhṛtaṃ purā
c śrutaṃ hṛdi ca nikṣiptaṃ nānyathā tad bhaviṣyati
a evaṃgate na saṃtāpaṃ gantum arhasi rāghava
c sītārthe rāghavārthe vā dṛḍho bhava narottama
a tac chrutvā vyāhṛtaṃ vākyaṃ sūtasya paramādbhutam
c praharṣam atulaṃ lebhe sādhu sādhv iti cābravīt
a tayoḥ saṃvadator evaṃ sūtalakṣmaṇayoḥ pathi
c astam arko gato vāsaṃ gomatyāṃ tāv athoṣatuḥ
a tatra tāṃ rajanīm uṣya gomatyāṃ raghunandanaḥ
c prabhāte punar utthāya lakṣmaṇaḥ prayayau tadā
a tato 'rdhadivase prāpte praviveśa mahārathaḥ
c ayodhyāṃ ratnasaṃpūrṇāṃ hṛṣṭapuṣṭajanāvṛtām
a saumitris tu paraṃ dainyaṃ jagāma sumahāmatiḥ
c rāmapādau samāsādya vakṣyāmi kim ahaṃ gataḥ
a tasyaivaṃ cintayānasya bhavanaṃ śaśisaṃnibham
c rājasya paramodāraṃ purastāt samadṛśyata
a rājñas tu bhavanadvāri so 'vatīrya narottamaḥ
c avānmukho dīnamanāḥ prāviveśānivāritaḥ
a sa dṛṣṭvā rāghavaṃ dīnam āsīnaṃ paramāsane
c netrābhyām aśrupūrṇābhyāṃ dadarśāgrajam agrataḥ
a jagrāha caraṇau tasya lakṣmaṇo dīnacetanaḥ
c uvāca dīnayā vācā prāñjaliḥ susamāhitaḥ
a āryasyājñāṃ puraskṛtya visṛjya janakātmajām
c gaṅgātīre yathoddiṣṭe vālmīker āśrame śubhe
e punar asmy āgato vīra pādamūlam upāsitum
a mā śucaḥ puruṣavyāghra kālasya gatir īdṛśī
c tvadvidhā na hi śocanti sattvavanto manasvinaḥ
a sarve kṣayāntā nicayāḥ patanāntāḥ samucchrayāḥ
c saṃyogā viprayogāntā maraṇāntaṃ ca jīvitam
a śaktas tvam ātmanātmānaṃ vijetuṃ manasaiva hi
c lokān sarvāṃś ca kākutstha kiṃ punar duḥkham īdṛśam
a nedṛśeṣu vimuhyanti tvadvidhāḥ puruṣarṣabhāḥ
c yadarthaṃ maithilī tyaktā apavādabhayān nṛpa
a sa tvaṃ puruṣaśārdūla dhairyeṇa susamāhitaḥ
c tyajemāṃ durbalāṃ buddhiṃ saṃtāpaṃ mā kuruṣva ha
a evam uktas tu kākutstho lakṣmaṇena mahātmanā
c uvāca parayā prītyā saumitriṃ mitravatsalam
a evam etan naraśreṣṭha yathā vadasi lakṣmaṇa
c paritoṣaś ca me vīra mama kāryānuśāsane
a nirvṛtiś ca kṛtā saumya saṃtāpaś ca nirākṛtaḥ
c bhavadvākyaiḥ sumadhurair anunīto 'smi lakṣmaṇa
a tataḥ sumantras tv āgamya rāghavaṃ vākyam abravīt
c ete nivāritā rājan dvāri tiṣṭhanti tāpasāḥ
a bhārgavaṃ cyavanaṃ nāma puraskṛtya maharṣayaḥ
c darśanaṃ te mahārāja codayanti kṛtatvarāḥ
e prīyamāṇā naravyāghra yamunātīravāsinaḥ
a tasya tadvacanaṃ śrutvā rāmaḥ provāca dharmavit
c praveśyantāṃ mahātmāno bhārgavapramukhā dvijāḥ
a rājñas tv ājñāṃ puraskṛtya dvāḥstho mūrdhni kṛtāñjaliḥ
c praveśayām āsa tatas tāpasān saṃmatān bahūn
a śataṃ samadhikaṃ tatra dīpyamānaṃ svatejasā
c praviṣṭaṃ rājabhavanaṃ tāpasānāṃ mahātmanām
a te dvijāḥ pūrṇakalaśaiḥ sarvatīrthāmbusatkṛtam
c gṛhītvā phalamūlaṃ ca rāmasyābhyāharan bahu
a pratigṛhya tu tat sarvaṃ rāmaḥ prītipuraskṛtaḥ
c tīrthodakāni sarvāṇi phalāni vividhāni ca
a uvāca ca mahābāhuḥ sarvān eva mahāmunīn
c imāny āsanamukhyāni yathārham upaviśyatām
a rāmasya bhāṣitaṃ śrutvā sarva eva maharṣayaḥ
c bṛsīṣu rucirākhyāsu niṣeduḥ kāñcanīṣu te
a upaviṣṭān ṛṣīṃs tatra dṛṣṭvā parapuraṃjayaḥ
c prayataḥ prāñjalir bhūtvā rāghavo vākyam abravīt
a kim āgamanakaryaṃ vaḥ kiṃ karomi tapodhanāḥ
c ājñāpyo 'haṃ maharṣīṇāṃ sarvakāmakaraḥ sukham
a idaṃ rājyaṃ ca sakalaṃ jīvitaṃ ca hṛdi sthitam
c sarvam etad dvijārthaṃ me satyam etad bravīmi vaḥ
a tasya tadvacanaṃ śrutvā sādhuvādo mahān abhūt
c ṛṣīṇām ugratapasāṃ yamunātīravāsinām
a ūcuś ca te mahātmāno harṣeṇa mahatānvitāḥ
c upapannaṃ naraśreṣṭha tavaiva bhuvi nānyataḥ
a bahavaḥ pārthivā rājann atikrāntā mahābalāḥ
c kāryagauravam aśrutvā pratijñāṃ nābhyarocayan
a tvayā punar brāhmaṇa gauravād iyaṃ
kṛtvā pratijñā hy anavekṣya kāraṇam
c kuruṣva kartā hy asi nātra saṃśayo
mahābhayāt trātum ṛṣīṃs tvam arhasi
a bruvadbhir evam ṛṣibhiḥ kākutstho vākyam abravīt
c kiṃ kāryaṃ brūta bhavatāṃ bhayaṃ nāśayitāsmi vaḥ
a tathā vadati kākutsthe bhargavo vākyam abravīt
c bhayaṃ naḥ śṛṇu yan mūlaṃ deśasya ca nareśvara
a pūrvaṃ kṛtayuge rāma daiteyaḥ sumahābalaḥ
c lolāputro 'bhavaj jyeṣṭho madhur nāma mahāsuraḥ
a brahmaṇyaś ca śaraṇyaś ca buddhyā ca pariniṣṭhitaḥ
c suraiś ca paramodāraiḥ prītis tasyātulābhavat
a sa madhur vīryasaṃpanno dharme ca susamāhitaḥ
c bahumānāc ca rudreṇa dattas tasyādbhuto varaḥ
a śūlaṃ śūlād viniṣkṛṣya mahāvīryaṃ mahāprabham
c dadau mahātmā suprīto vākayṃ caitad uvāca ha
a tvayāyam atulo dharmo matprasādāt kṛtaḥ śubhaḥ
c prītyā paramayā yukto dadāmy āyudham uttamam
a yāvat suraiś ca vipraiś ca na virudhyer mahāsura
c tāvac chūlaṃ tavedaṃ syād anyathā nāśam āpnuyāt
a yaś ca tvām abhiyuñjīta yuddhāya vigatajvaraḥ
c taṃ śūlaṃ bhasmasāt kṛtvā punar eṣyati te karam
a evaṃ rudrād varaṃ labdhvā bhūya eva mahāsuraḥ
c praṇipatya mahādevaṃ vākyam etad uvāca ha
a bhagavan mama vaṃśasya śūlam etad anuttamam
c bhavet tu satataṃ deva surāṇām īśvaro hy asi
a taṃ bruvāṇaṃ madhuṃ devaḥ sarvabhūtapatiḥ śivaḥ
c pratyuvāca mahādevo naitad evaṃ bhaviṣyati
a mā bhūt te viphalā bāṇī matprāsādakṛtā śubhā
c bhavataḥ putram ekaṃ tu śūlam etad gamiṣyati
a yāvat karasthaḥ śūlo 'yaṃ bhaviṣyati sutasya te
c avadhyaḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ śūlahasto bhaviṣyati
a evaṃ madhuvaraṃ labdhvā devāt sumahad adbhutam
c bhavanaṃ cāsuraśreṣṭhaḥ kārayām āsa suprabham
a tasya patnī mahābhagā priyā kumbhīnasī hi yā
c viśvāsayor apatyaṃ sā hy analāyāṃ mahāprabhā
a tasyāḥ putro mahāvīryo lavaṇo nāma dāruṇaḥ
c bālyāt prabhṛti duṣṭātmā pāpāny eva samācarat
a taṃ putraṃ durvinītaṃ tu dṛṣṭvā duḥkhasamanvitaḥ
c madhuḥ sa śokam āpede na cainaṃ kiṃ cid abravīt
a sa vihāya imaṃ lokaṃ praviṣṭo varuṇālayam
c śūlaṃ niveśya lavaṇe varaṃ tasmai nyavedayat
a sa prabhāvena śūlasya daurātmyenātmanas tathā
c saṃtāpayati lokāṃs trīn viśeṣeṇa tu tāpasān
a evaṃprabhāvo lavaṇaḥ śūlaṃ caiva tathāvidham
c śrutvā pramāṇaṃ kākutsthaṃ tvaṃ hi naḥ paramā gatiḥ
a bahavaḥ pārthivā rāma bhayārtair ṛṣibhiḥ purā
c abhayaṃ yācitā vīra trātāraṃ na ca vidmahe
a te vayaṃ rāvaṇaṃ śrutvā hataṃ sabalavāhanam
c trātāraṃ vidmahe rāma nānyaṃ bhuvi narādhipam
e tat paritrātum icchāmo lavaṇād bhayapīḍitāḥ
a tathokte tān ṛṣīn rāmaḥ pratyuvāca kṛtāñjaliḥ
c kimāhāraḥ kimācāro lavaṇaḥ kva ca vartate
a rāghavasya vacaḥ śrutvā ṛṣayaḥ sarva eva te
c tato nivedayām āsur lavaṇo vavṛdhe yathā
a āhāraḥ sarvasattvāni viśeṣeṇa ca tāpasāḥ
c ācāro raudratā nityaṃ vāso madhuvane sadā
a hatvā daśasahasrāṇi siṃhavyāghramṛgadvipān
c mānuṣāṃś caiva kurute nityam āhāram āhnikam
a tato 'parāṇi sattvāni khādate sa mahābalaḥ
c saṃhāre samanuprāpte vyāditāsya ivāntakaḥ
a tac chrutvā rāghavo vākyam uvāca sa mahāmunīn
c ghātayiṣyāmi tad rakṣo vyapagacchatu vo bhayam
a tathā teṣāṃ pratijñāya munīnām ugratejasām
c sa bhrātṝn sahitān sarvān uvāca raghunandanaḥ
a ko hantā lavaṇaṃ vīrāḥ kasyāṃśaḥ sa vidhīyatām
c bharatasya mahābāhoḥ śatrughnasyāthavā punaḥ
a rāghaveṇaivam uktas tu bharato vākyam abravīt
c aham enaṃ badhiṣyāmi mamāṃśaḥ sa vidhīyatām
a bharatasya vacaḥ śrutvā śauryavīryasamanvitam
c lakṣmaṇāvarajas tasthau hitvā sauvarṇam āsanam
a śatrughnas tv abravīd vākyaṃ praṇipatya narādhipam
c kṛtakarmā mahābāhur madhyamo raghunandanaḥ
a āryeṇa hi purā śūnyā ayodhyā rakṣitā purī
c saṃtāpaṃ hṛdaye kṛtvā āryasyāgamanaṃ prati
a duḥkhāni ca bahūnīha anubhūtāni pārthiva
c śayāno duḥkhaśayyāsu nandigrāme mahātmanā
a phalamūlāśano bhūtvā jaṭācīradharas tathā
c anubhūyedṛśaṃ duḥkham eṣa rāghavanandanaḥ
e preṣye mayi sthite rājan na bhūyaḥ kleśam āpnuyāt
a tathā bruvati śatrughne rāghavaḥ punar abravīt
c evaṃ bhavatu kākutstha kriyatāṃ mama śāsanam
a rājye tvām abhiṣekṣyāmi maghos tu nagare śubhe
c niveśaya mahābāho bharataṃ yady avekṣase
a śūras tvaṃ kṛtavidyaś ca samarthaḥ saṃniveśane
c nagaraṃ madhunā juṣṭaṃ tathā janapadāñ śubhān
a yo hi vaṃśaṃ samutpāṭya pārthivasya punaḥ kṣaye
c na vidhatte nṛpaṃ tatra narakaṃ sa nigacchati
a sa tvaṃ hatvā madhusutaṃ lavaṇaṃ pāpaniścayam
c rājyaṃ praśādhi dharmeṇa vākyaṃ me yady avekṣase
a uttaraṃ ca na vaktavyaṃ śūra vākyāntare mama
c bālena pūrvajasyājñā kartavyā nātra saṃśayaḥ
a abhiṣekaṃ ca kākutstha pratīcchasva mayodyatam
c vasiṣṭhapramukhair viprair vidhimantrapuraskṛtam
a evam uktas tu rāmeṇa parāṃ vrīḍām upāgataḥ
c śatrughno vīryasaṃpanno mandaṃ mandam uvāca ha
a avaśyaṃ karaṇīyaṃ ca śāsanaṃ puruṣarṣabha
c tava caiva mahābhāga śāsanaṃ duratikramam
e ayaṃ kāmakaro rājaṃs tavāsmi puruṣarṣabha
a evam ukte tu śūreṇa śatrughnena mahātmanā
c uvāca rāmaḥ saṃhṛṣṭo lakṣmaṇaṃ bharataṃ tathā
a saṃbhārān abhiṣekasya ānayadhvaṃ samāhitāḥ
c adyaiva puruṣavyāghram abhiṣekṣyāmi durjayam
a purodhasaṃ ca kākutsthau naigamān ṛtvijas tathā
c mantriṇaś caiva me sarvān ānayadhvaṃ mamājñayā
a rājñaḥ śāsanam ājñāya tathākurvan mahārathaḥ
c abhiṣekasamārambhaṃ puraskṛtya purodhasaṃ
e praviṣṭā rājabhavanaṃ puraṃdara gṛhopamam
a tato 'bhiṣeko vavṛdhe śatrughnasya mahātmanaḥ
c saṃpraharṣakaraḥ śrīmān rāghavasya purasya ca
a tato 'bhiṣiktaṃ śatrughnam aṅkam āropya rāghavaḥ
c uvāca madhurāṃ vāṇīṃ tejas tasyābhipūrayan
a ayaṃ śaras tv amoghas te divyaḥ parapuraṃjayaḥ
c anena lavaṇaṃ saumya hantāsi raghunandana
a sṛṣṭaḥ śaro 'yaṃ kākutstha yadā śete mahārṇave
c svayambhūr ajito devo yaṃ nāpaśyan surāsurāḥ
a adṛśyaḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ tenāyaṃ hi śarottamaḥ
c sṛṣṭaḥ krodhābhibhūtena vināśārthaṃ durātmanoḥ
e madhukauṭabhayor vīra vighāte vartamānayoḥ
a sraṣṭukāmena lokāṃs trīṃs tau cānena hatau yudhi
c anena śaramukhyena tato lokāṃś cakāra saḥ
a nāyaṃ mayā śaraḥ pūrvaṃ rāvaṇasya vadhārthinā
c mukhaḥ śatrughna bhūtānāṃ mahāṃs trāso bhaved iti
a yac ca tasya mahac chūlaṃ tryambakeṇa mahātmanā
c dattaṃ śatruvināśāya madhor āyudham uttamam
a tat saṃnikṣipya bhavane pūjyamānaṃ punaḥ punaḥ
c diśaḥ sarvāḥ samālokya prāpnoty āhāram ātmanaḥ
a yadā tu yuddham ākāṅkṣan kaś cid enaṃ samāhvayet
c tadā śūlaṃ gṛhītvā tad bhasma rakṣaḥ karoti tam
a sa tvaṃ puruṣaśārdūla tam āyudhavivarjitam
c apraviṣṭapuraṃ pūrvaṃ dvāri tiṣṭha dhṛtāyudhaḥ
a apraviṣṭaṃ ca bhavanaṃ yuddhāya puruṣarṣabha
c āhvayethā mahābāho tato hantāsi rākṣasaṃ
a anyathā kriyamāṇe tu avadhyaḥ sa bhaviṣyati
c yadi tv evaṃ kṛte vīra vināśam upayāsyati
a etat te sarvam ākhyātaṃ śūlasya ca viparyayam
c śrīmataḥ śitikaṇṭhasya kṛtyaṃ hi duratikramam
a evam uktvā tu kākutsthaṃ praśasya ca punaḥ punaḥ
c punar evāparaṃ vākyam uvāca raghunandanaḥ
a imāny aśvasahasrāṇi catvāri puruṣarṣabha
c rathānāṃ ca sahasre dve gajānāṃ śatam eva ca
a antarāpaṇavīthyaś ca nānāpaṇyopaśobhitāḥ
c anugacchantu śatrughna tathaiva naṭanartakāḥ
a hiraṇyasya suvarṇasya ayutaṃ puruṣarṣabha
c gṛhītvā gaccha śatrughna paryāptadhanavāhanaḥ
a balaṃ ca subhṛtaṃ vīra hṛṣṭapuṣṭam anuttamam
c saṃbhāṣya saṃpradānena rañjayasva narottama
a na hy arthās tatra tiṣṭhanti na dārā na ca bāndhavāḥ
c suprīto bhṛtyavargas tu yatra tiṣṭhati rāghava
a ato hṛṣṭajanākīrṇāṃ prasthāpya mahatīṃ camūm
c eka eva dhanuṣpānis tad gaccha tvaṃ madhor vanam
a yathā tvāṃ na prajānāti gacchantaṃ yuddhakāṅkṣiṇam
c lavaṇas tu madhoḥ putras tathā gaccher aśaṅkitaḥ
a na tasya mṛtyur anyo 'sti kaścid dhi puruṣarṣabha
c darśanaṃ yo 'bhigaccheta sa vadhyo lavaṇena hi
a sa grīṣme vyapayāte tu varṣarātra upasthite
c hanyās tvaṃ lavaṇaṃ saumya sa hi kālo 'sya durmateḥ
a maharṣīṃs tu puraskṛtya prayāntu tava sainikāḥ
c yathā grīṣmāvaśeṣeṇa tareyur jāhnavījalam
a tataḥ sthāpya balaṃ sarvaṃ nadītīre samāhitaḥ
c agrato dhanuṣā sārdhaṃ gaccha tvaṃ laghuvikrama
a evam uktas tu rāmeṇa śatrughnas tān mahābalān
c senāmukhyān samānīya tato vākyam uvāca ha
a ete vo gaṇitā vāsā yatra yatra nivatsyatha
c sthātavyaṃ cāvirodhena yathā bādhā na kasya cit
a tathā tāṃs tu samājñāpya niryāpya ca mahad balam
c kausalyāṃ ca sumitrāṃ ca kaukeyīṃ cābhyavādayat
a rāmaṃ pradakṣiṇaṃ kṛtvā śirasābhipraṇamya ca
c rāṇeṇa cābhyanujñātaḥ śatrughnaḥ śatrutāpanaḥ
a lakṣmaṇaṃ bharataṃ caiva praṇipatya kṛtāñjaliḥ
c purodhasaṃ vasiṣṭhaṃ ca śatrughnaḥ prayatātmavān
e pradakṣiṇam atho kṛtvā nirjagāma mahābalaḥ
a prasthāpya tad balaṃ sarvaṃ māsamātroṣitaḥ pathi
c eka evāśu śatrughno jagāma tvaritas tadā
a dvirātram antare śūra uṣya rāghavanandanaḥ
c vālmīker āśramaṃ puṇyam agacchad vāsam uttamam
a so 'bhivādya mahātmānaṃ vālmīkiṃ munisattamam
c kṛtāñjalir atho bhūtvā vākyam etad uvāca ha
a bhagavan vastum icchāmi guroḥ kṛtyād ihāgataḥ
c śvaḥ prabhāte gamiṣyāmi pratīcīṃ vāruṇīṃ diśam
a śatrughnasya vacaḥ śrutvā prahasya munipuṃgavaḥ
c pratyuvaca mahātmānaṃ svāgataṃ te mahāyaśaḥ
a svam āśramam idaṃ saumya rāghavāṇāṃ kulasya ha
c āsanaṃ pādyam arghyaṃ ca nirviśaṅkaḥ pratīccha me
a pratigṛhya tataḥ pūjāṃ phalamūlaṃ ca bhojanam
c bhakṣayām āsa kākutsthas tṛptiṃ ca paramāṃ gataḥ
a sa tu bhuktvā mahābāhur maharṣiṃ tam uvāca ha
c pūrvaṃ yajñavibhūtīyaṃ kasyāśramasamīpataḥ
a tasya tadbhāṣitaṃ śrutvā vālmīkir vākyam abravīt
c śatrughna śṛṇu yasyedaṃ babhūvāyatanaṃ purā
a yuṣmākaṃ pūrvako rājā sudāsasya mahātmanaḥ
c putro mitrasaho nāma vīryavān atidhārmikaḥ
a sa bāla eva saudāso mṛgayām upacakrame
c cañcūryamāṇaṃ dadṛśe sa śūro rākṣasadvayam
a śārdūlarūpiṇau ghorau mṛgān bahusahasraśaḥ
c bhakṣayāṇāv asaṃtuṣṭau paryāptiṃ ca na jagmatuḥ
a sa tu tau rākṣasau dṛṣṭvā nirmṛgaṃ ca vanaṃ kṛtam
c krodhena mahatāviṣṭo jaghānaikaṃ maheṣuṇā
a vinipātya tam ekaṃ tu saudāsaḥ puruṣarṣabhaḥ
c vijvaro vigatāmarṣo hataṃ rakṣo 'bhyavaikṣata
a nirīkṣamāṇaṃ taṃ dṛṣṭvā sahāyas tasya rakṣasaḥ
c saṃtāpam akarod ghoraṃ saudāsaṃ cedam abravīt
a yasmād anaparāddhaṃ tvaṃ sahāyaṃ mama jaghnivān
c tasmāt tavāpu pāpiṣṭha pradāsyāmi pratikriyām
a evam uktvā tu taṃ rakṣas tatraivāntaradhīyata
c kālaparyāya yogena rājā mitrasaho 'bhavat
a rājāpi yajate yajñaṃ tasyāśramasamīpataḥ
c aśvamedhaṃ mahāyajñaṃ taṃ vasiṣṭho 'bhyapālayat
a tatra yajño mahān āsīd bahuvarṣa gaṇāyutān
c samṛddhaḥ parayā lakṣmyā devayajñasamo 'bhavat
a athāvasāne yajñasya pūrvavairam anusmaran
c vasiṣṭharūpī rājānam iti hovāca rākṣasaḥ
a adya yajñāvasānānte sāmiṣaṃ bhojanaṃ mama
c dīyatām iti śīghraṃ vai nātra kāryā vicāraṇā
a tac chrutvā vyāhṛtaṃ vākyaṃ rakṣasā kāmarūpiṇā
c bhakṣasaṃskārakuśalam uvāca pṛthivīpatiḥ
a haviṣyaṃ sāmiṣaṃ svādu yathā bhavati bhojanam
c tathā kuruṣva śīghraṃ vai parituṣyed yathā guruḥ
a śāsanāt pārthivendrasya sūdaḥ saṃbhrāntamānasaḥ
c sa ca rakṣaḥ punas tatra sūdaveṣam athākarot
a sa mānuṣam atho māṃsaṃ pārthivāya nyavedayat
c idaṃ svāduhaviṣyaṃ ca sāmiṣaṃ cānnam āhṛtam
a sa bhojanaṃ vasiṣṭhāya patnyā sārdham upāharat
c madayantyā naravyāghra sāmiṣaṃ rakṣasā hṛtam
a jñātvā tadāmiṣaṃ vipro mānuṣaṃ bhojanāhṛtam
c krodhena mahatāviṣṭo vyāhartum upacakrame
a yasmāt tvaṃ bhojanaṃ rājan mamaitad dātum icchasi
c tasmād bhojanam etat te bhaviṣyati na saṃśayaḥ
a sa rājā saha patnyā vai praṇipatya muhur muhuḥ
c punar vasiṣṭhaṃ provāca yad uktaṃ brahmarūpiṇā
a tac chrutā pārthivendrasya rakṣasā vikṛtaṃ ca tat
c punaḥ provāca rājānaṃ vasiṣṭhaḥ puruṣarṣabham
a mayā roṣaparītena yad idaṃ vyāhṛtaṃ vacaḥ
c naitac chakyaṃ vṛthā kartuṃ pradāsyāmi ca te varam
a kālo dvādaśa varṣāṇi śāpasyāsya bhaviṣyati
c matprasādāc ca rājendra atītaṃ na smariṣyasi
a evaṃ sa rājā taṃ śāpam upabhujyārimardanaḥ
c pratilebhe punā rājyaṃ prajāś caivānvapālayat
a tasya kalmāṣapādasya yajñasyāyatanaṃ śubham
c āśramasya samīpe 'smin yasmin pṛcchasi rāghava
a tasya tāṃ pārthivendrasya kathāṃ śrutvā sudāruṇam
c viveśa parṇaśālāyāṃ maharṣim abhivādya ca
a yām eva rātriṃ śatrughna parṇaśālāṃ samāviśat
c tām eva rātriṃ sītāpi prasūtā dārakadvayam
a tato 'rdharātrasamaye bālakā munidārakāḥ
c vālmīkeḥ priyam ācakhyuḥ sītāyāḥ prasavaṃ śubham
e tasya rakṣāṃ mahātejaḥ kuru bhūtavināśinīm
a teṣāṃ tad vacanaṃ śrutvā munir harṣam upāgamat
c bhūtaghnīṃ cākarot tābhyā rakṣāṃ rakṣovināśinīm
a kuśamuṣṭim upādāya lavaṃ caiva tu sa dvijaḥ
c vālmīkiḥ pradadau tābhyāṃ rakṣāṃ bhūtavināśinīm
a yas tayoḥ pūrvajo jātaḥ sa kuśair mantrasaṃskṛtaiḥ
c nirmārjanīyas tu bhavet kuśa ity asya nāmataḥ
a yaś cāparo bhavet tābhyāṃ lavena susamāhitaḥ
c nirmārjanīyo vṛddhābhir lavaś ceti sa nāmataḥ
a evaṃ kuśalavau nāmnā tāv ubhau yamajātakau
c matkṛtabhyāṃ ca namābhyāṃ khyātiyuktau bhaviṣyataḥ
a te rakṣāṃ jagṛhus tāṃ ca munihastāt samāhitāḥ
c akurvaṃś ca tato rakṣāṃ tayor vigatakalmaṣāḥ
a tathā tāṃ kriyamāṇāṃ tu rakṣāṃ gotraṃ ca nāma ca
c saṃkīrtanaṃ ca rāmasya sītāyāḥ prasavau śubhau
a ardharātre tu śatrughnaḥ śuśrāva sumahat priyam
c parṇaśālāṃ gato rātrau diṣṭyā diṣṭyeti cābravīt
a tatha tasya prahṛṣṭasya śatrughnasya mahātmanaḥ
c vyatītā vārṣikī rātriḥ śrāvaṇī laghuvikramā
a prabhāte tu mahāvīryaḥ kṛtvā paurvāhṇikaṃ kramam
c muniṃ prāñjalir āmantrya prāyāt paścānmukhaḥ punaḥ
a sa gatvā yamunātīraṃ saptarātroṣitaḥ pathi
c ṛṣīṇāṃ puṇyakīrtīnām āśrame vāsam abhyayāt
a sa tatra munibhiḥ sārdhaṃ bhārgavapramukhair nṛpaḥ
c kathābhir bahurūpābhir vāsaṃ cakre mahāyaśāḥ
a atha rātryāṃ pravṛttāyāṃ śatrughno bhṛgunandanam
c papraccha cyavanaṃ vipraṃ lavaṇasya balābalam
a śūlasya ca balaṃ brahman ke ca pūrvaṃ nipātitāḥ
c anena śūlamukhena dvandvayuddham upāgatāḥ
a tasya tadbhāṣitaṃ śrutvā śatrughnasya mahātmanaḥ
c pratyuvāca mahātejāś cyavano raghunandanam
a asaṃkhyeyāni karmāṇi yāny asya puruṣarṣabha
c ikṣvākuvaṃśaprabhave yad vṛttaṃ tac chṛṇuṣva me
a ayodhyāyāṃ purā rājā yuvanāśvasuto balī
c māndhatā iti vikhyātas triṣu lokeṣu vīryavān
a sa kṛtvā pṛthivīṃ kṛtsnāṃ śāsane pṛthivīpatiḥ
c suralokam atho jetum udyogam akaron nṛpaḥ
a indrasya tu bhayaṃ tīvraṃ surāṇāṃ ca mahātmanām
c māndhātari kṛtodyoge devalokajigīṣayā
a ardhāsanena śakrasya rājyārdhena ca pārthivaḥ
c vandyamānaḥ suragaṇaiḥ pratijñām adhyarohata
a tasya pāpam abhiprāyaṃ viditvā pākaśāsanaḥ
c sāntvapūrvam idaṃ vākyam uvāca yuvanāśvajam
a rājā tvaṃ mānuṣaṃ loke na tāvat puruṣarṣabha
c akṛtvā pṛthivīṃ vaśyāṃ devarājyam ihecchasi
a yadi vīra samagrā te medinī nikhilā vaśe
c devarājyaṃ kuruṣveha sabhṛtyabalavāhanaḥ
a indram evaṃ bruvāṇaṃ tu māndhātā vākyam abravīt
c kva me śakrapratihataṃ śāsanaṃ pṛthivītale
a tam uvāca sahasrākṣo lavaṇo nāma rākṣasaḥ
c madhuputro madhuvane nājñāṃ te kurute 'nagha
a tac chrutvā vipriyaṃ ghoraṃ sahasrākṣeṇa bhāṣitam
c vrīḍito 'vāṅmukho rājā vyāhartuṃ na śaśāka ha
a āmantrya tu sahasrākṣaṃ hriyā kiṃ cid avāṅmukhaḥ
c punar evāgamac chrīmān imaṃ lokaṃ nareśvaraḥ
a sa kṛtvā hṛdaye 'marṣaṃ sabhṛtyabalavāhanaḥ
c ājagāma madhoḥ putraṃ vaśe kartum aninditaḥ
a sa kāṅkṣamāṇo lavaṇaṃ yuddhāya puruṣarṣabhaḥ
c dūtaṃ saṃpreṣayām āsa sakāśaṃ lavaṇasya saḥ
a sa gatvā vipriyāṇy āha bahūni madhunaḥ sutam
c vadantam evaṃ taṃ dūtaṃ bhakṣayām āsa rākṣasaḥ
a cirāyamāṇe dūte tu rājā krodhasamanvitaḥ
c ardayām āsa tad rakṣaḥ śaravṛṣṭyā samantataḥ
a tataḥ prahasya lavaṇaḥ śūlaṃ jagrāha pāṇinā
c vadhāya sānubandhasya mumocāyudham uttamam
a tac chūlaṃ dīpyamānaṃ tu sabhṛtyabalavāhanam
c bhasmīkṛtya nṛpaṃ bhūyo lavaṇasyāgamat karam
a evaṃ sa rājā sumahān hataḥ sabalavāhanaḥ
c śūlasya ca balaṃ vīra aprameyam anuttamam
a śvaḥ prabhāte tu lavaṇaṃ vadhiṣyasi na saṃśayaḥ
c agṛhītāyudhaṃ kṣipraṃ dhruvo hi vijayas tava
a kathāṃ kathayatāṃ teṣāṃ jayaṃ cākāṅkṣatāṃ śubham
c vyatītā rajanī śīghraṃ śatrughnasya mahātmanaḥ
a tataḥ prabhāte vimale tasmin kāle sa rākṣasaḥ
c nirgatas tu purād vīro bhakṣāhārapracoditaḥ
a etasminn antare śūraḥ śatrughno yamunāṃ nadīm
c tīrtvā madhupuradvāri dhanuṣpāṇir atiṣṭhata
a tato 'rdhadivase prāpte krūrakarmā sa rākṣasaḥ
c āgacchad bahusahasraṃ prāṇinām udvahan bharam
a tato dadarśa śatrughnaṃ sthitaṃ dvāri dhṛtāyudham
c tam uvāca tato rakṣaḥ kim anena kariṣyasi
a īdṛśānāṃ sahasrāṇi sāyudhānāṃ narādhama
c bhakṣitāni mayā roṣāt kālam ākāṅkṣase nu kim
a āhāraś cāpy asaṃpūrṇo mamāyaṃ puruṣādhama
c svayaṃ praviṣṭo nu mukhaṃ katham āsādya durmate
a tasyaivaṃ bhāṣamāṇasya hasataś ca muhur muhuḥ
c śatrughno vīryasaṃpanno roṣād aśrūṇy avartayat
a tasya roṣābhibhūtasya śatrughnasya mahātmanaḥ
c tejomayā marīcyas tu sarvagātrair viniṣpatan
a uvāca ca susaṃkruddhaḥ śatrughnas taṃ niśācaram
c yoddhum icchāmi durbuddhe dvandvayuddhaṃ tvayā saha
a putro daśarathasyāhaṃ bhrātā rāmasya dhīmataḥ
c śatrughno nāma śatrughno vadhākāṅkṣī tavāgataḥ
a tasya me yuddhakāmasya dvandvayuddhaṃ pradīyatām
c śatrus tvaṃ sarvajīvānāṃ na me jīvan gamiṣyasi
a tasmiṃs tathā bruvāṇe tu rākṣasaḥ prahasann iva
c pratyuvāca naraśreṣṭhaṃ diṣṭyā prāpto 'si durmate
a mama mātṛṣvasur bhrātā rāvaṇo nāma rākṣasaḥ
c hato rāmeṇa durbuddhe strīhetoḥ puruṣādhama
a tac ca sarvaṃ mayā kṣāntaṃ rāvaṇasyā kulakṣayam
c avajñāṃ purataḥ kṛtvā mayā yūyaṃ viśeṣataḥ
a na hatāś ca hi me sarve paribhūtās tṛṇaṃ yathā
c bhūtaś caiva bhaviṣyāś ca yūyaṃ ca puruṣādhamāḥ
a tasya te yuddhakāmasyā yuddhaṃ dāsyāmi durmate
c īpsitaṃ yādṛśaṃ tubhyaṃ sajjaye yāvad āyudham
a tam uvācātha śatrughna kva me jīvan gamiṣyasi
c durbalo 'py āgataḥ śatrur na moktavyaḥ kṛtātmanā
a yo hi viklavayā buddhyā prasaraṃ śatrave dadau
c sa hato mandabuddhitvād yathā kāpuruṣas tathā
a tac chrutvā bhāṣitaṃ tasya śatrughnasya mahātmanaḥ
c krodham āhārayat tīvraṃ tiṣṭha tiṣṭheti cābravīt
a pāṇau pāṇiṃ viniṣpiṣya dantān kaṭakaṭāyya ca
c lavaṇo raghuśārdūlam āhvayām āsa cāsakṛt
a taṃ bruvāṇaṃ tathā vākyaṃ lavaṇaṃ ghoravikramam
c śatrughno deva śatrughna idaṃ vacanam abravīt
a śatrughno na tadā jāto yadānye nirjitās tvayā
c tad adya bāṇābhihato vraja taṃ yamasādanam
a ṛṣayo 'py adya pāpātman mayā tvāṃ nihataṃ raṇe
c paśyantu viprā vidvāṃsas tridaśā iva rāvaṇam
a tvayi madbāṇanirdagdhe patite 'dya niśācara
c puraṃ janapadaṃ cāpi kṣemam etad bhaviṣyati
a adya madbāhuniṣkrāntaḥ śaro vajranibhānanaḥ
c pravekṣyate te hṛdayaṃ padmam aṃśur ivārkajaḥ
a evam ukto mahāvṛkṣaṃ lavaṇaḥ krodhamūrchitaḥ
c śatrughnorasi cikṣepa taṃ śūraḥ śatadhācchinat
a tad dṛṣṭvā viphalaṃ karma rākṣasaḥ punar eva tu
c pādapān subahūn gṛhya śatrughne vyasṛjad balī
a śatrughnaś cāpi tejasvī vṛkṣān āpatato bahūn
c tribhiś caturbhir ekaikaṃ ciccheda nataparvabhiḥ
a tato bāṇamayaṃ varṣaṃ vyasṛjad rākṣasor asi
c śatrughno vīryasaṃpanno vivyathe na ca rākṣasaḥ
a tataḥ prahasya lavaṇo vṛkṣam utpāṭya līlayā
c śirasy abhyahanac chūraṃ srastāṅgaḥ sa mumoha vai
a tasmin nipatite vīre hāhākāro mahān abhūt
c ṛṣīṇāṃ deva saṃghānāṃ gandharvāpsarasām api
a tam avajñāya tu hataṃ śatrughnaṃ bhuvi pātitam
c rakṣo labdhāntaram api na viveśa svam ālayam
a nāpi śūlaṃ prajagrāha taṃ dṛṣṭvā bhuvi pātitam
c tato hata iti jñātvā tān bhakṣān samudāvahat
a muhūrtāl labdhasaṃjñas tu punas tasthau dhṛtāyudhaḥ
c śatrughno rākṣasadvāri ṛṣibhiḥ saṃprapūjitaḥ
a tato divyam amoghaṃ taṃ jagrāha śaram uttamam
c jvalantaṃ tejasā ghoraṃ pūrayantaṃ diśo daśa
a vajrānanaṃ vajravegaṃ merumandara gauravam
c nataṃ parvasu sarveṣu saṃyugeṣv aparājitam
a asṛkcandanadigdhāṅgaṃ cārupatraṃ patatriṇam
c dānavendrācalendrāṇām asurāṇāṃ ca dāruṇam
a taṃ dīptam iva kālāgniṃ yugānte samupasthite
c dṛṣṭvā sarvāṇi bhūtāni paritrāsam upāgaman
a sadevāsuragandharvaṃ samuniṃ sāpsarogaṇam
c jagad dhi sarvam asvasthaṃ pitāmaham upasthitam
a ūcuś ca devadeveśaṃ varadaṃ prapitāmaham
c kaccil lokakṣayo deva prāpto vā yugasaṃkayaḥ
a nedṛśaṃ dṛṣṭapūrvaṃ na śrutaṃ vā prapitāmaha
c devānāṃ bhayasaṃmoho lokānāṃ saṃkṣayaḥ prabho
a teṣāṃ tad vacanaṃ śrutvā brahmā lokapitāmanaḥ
c bhayakāraṇam ācaṣṭe devānām abhayaṃkaraḥ
a vadhāya lavaṇasyājau śaraḥ śatrughnadhāritaḥ
c tejasā yasya sarve sma saṃmūḍhāḥ surasattamāḥ
a eṣo hi pūrvaṃ devasya lokakartuḥ sanātanaḥ
c śaras tejomayo vatsā yena vai bhayam āgatam
a eṣa vai kaiṭabhasyārthe madhunaś ca mahāśaraḥ
c sṛṣṭo mahātmanā tena vadhārthaṃ daityayos tayoḥ
a evam etaṃ prajānīdhvaṃ viṣṇos tejomayaṃ śaram
c eṣā caiva tanuḥ pūrvā viṣṇos tasya mahātmanaḥ
a ito gacchatā paśyadhvaṃ vadhyamānaṃ mahātmanā
c rāmānujena vīreṇa lavaṇaṃ rākṣasottamam
a tasya te devadevasya niśamya madhurāṃ giram
c ājagmur yatra yudhyete śatrughnalavaṇāv ubhau
a taṃ śaraṃ divyasaṃkāśaṃ śatrughnakaradhāritam
c dadṛśuḥ sarvabhūtāni yugāntāgnim ivotthitam
a ākāśam āvṛtaṃ dṛṣṭvā devair hi raghunandanaḥ
c siṃhanādaṃ muhuḥ kṛtvā dadarśa lavaṇaṃ punaḥ
a āhūtaś ca tatas tena śatrughnena mahātmanā
c lavaṇaḥ krodhasaṃyukto yuddhāya samupasthitaḥ
a ākarṇāt sa vikṛṣyātha tad dhanur dhanvināṃ varaḥ
c sa mumoca mahābāṇaṃ lavaṇasya mahorasi
e uras tasya vidāryāśu praviveśa rasātalam
a gatvā rasātalaṃ divyaṃ śaro vibudhapūjitaḥ
c punar evāgamat tūrṇam ikṣvākukulanandanam
a śatrughnaśaranirbhinno lavaṇaḥ sa niśācaraḥ
c papāta sahasā bhūmau vajrāhata ivācalaḥ
a tac ca divyaṃ mahac chūlaṃ hate lavaṇarākṣase
c paśyatāṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ rudrasya vaśam anvagāt
a ekeṣupātena bhayaṃ nihatya
lokatrayasyāsya raghupravīraḥ
c vinirbabhāv udyatacāpabāṇas
tamaḥ praṇudyeva sahasraraśmiḥ
a hate tu lavaṇe devāḥ sendrāḥ sāgnipurogamāḥ
c ūcuḥ sumadhurāṃ vāṇīṃ śatrughnāṃ śatrutāpanam
a diṣṭyā te vijayo vatsa diṣṭya lavaṇarākṣasaḥ
c hataḥ puruṣaśārdūlavaraṃ varaya rāghava
a varadāḥ sma mahābāho sarva eva samāgatāḥ
c vijayākāṅkṣiṇas tubhyam amoghaṃ darśanaṃ hi naḥ
a devānāṃ bhāṣitaṃ śrutvā śūro mūrdhni kṛtāñjaliḥ
c pratyuvāca mahābāhuḥ śatrughnaḥ prayatātmavān
a imāṃ madhupurīṃ ramyāṃ madhurāṃ deva nirmitām
c niveśaṃ prapnuyāṃ śīghram eṣa me 'stu varo mataḥ
a taṃ devāḥ prītamanaso bāḍham ity eva rāghavam
c bhaviṣyati purī ramyā śūrasenā na saṃśayaḥ
a te tathoktvā mahātmāno divam āruruhus tadā
c śatrughno 'pi mahātejās tāṃ senāṃ samupānayat
a sā sena śīghram āgacchac chrutvā śatrughnaśāsanam
c niveśanaṃ ca śatrughnaḥ śāsanena samārabhat
a sā purī divyasaṃkāśā varṣe dvādaśame śubhā
c niviṣṭā śūrasenānāṃ viṣayaś cākutobhayaḥ
a kṣetrāṇi sasya yuktāni kāle varṣati vāsavaḥ
c arogā vīrapuruṣā śatrughnabhujapālitā
a ardhacandrapratīkāśā yamunātīraśobhitā
c śobhitā gṛhamukhyaiś ca śobhitā catvarāpaṇaiḥ
a yac ca tena mahac chūnyaṃ lavaṇena kṛtaṃ purā
c śobhayām āsa tad vīro nānāpaṇyasamṛddhibhiḥ
a tāṃ samṛddhāṃ samṛddhārthaḥ śatrughno bharatānujaḥ
c nirīkṣya paramaprītaḥ paraṃ harṣam upāgamat
a tasya buddhiḥ samutpannā niveśya madhurāṃ purīm
c rāmapādau nirīkṣeyaṃ varṣe dvādaśame śubhe
a tato dvādaśame varṣe śatrughno rāmapālitām
c ayodhyāṃ cakame gantum alpabhṛtyabalānugaḥ
a mantriṇo balamukhyāṃś ca nivartya ca purodhasaṃ
c jagāma rathamukhyena hayayuktena bhāsvatā
a sa gatvā gaṇitān vāsān saptāṣṭau raghunandanaḥ
c ayodhyām agamat tūrṇaṃ rāghavotsukadarśanaḥ
a sa praviśya purīṃ ramyāṃ śrīmān ikṣvākunandanaḥ
c praviveśa mahābāhur yatra rāmo mahādyutiḥ
a so 'bhivādya mahātmānaṃ jvalantam iva tejasā
c uvāca prāñjalir bhūtvā rāmaṃ satyaparākramam
a yad ājñaptaṃ mahārāja sarvaṃ tat kṛtavān aham
c hataḥ sa lavaṇaḥ pāpaḥ purī sā ca niveśitā
a dvādaśaṃ ca gataṃ varṣaṃ tvāṃ vinā raghunandana
c notsaheyam ahaṃ vastuṃ tvayā virahito nṛpa
a sa me prasādaṃ kākutstha kuruṣvāmitavikrama
c mātṛhīno yathā vatsas tvāṃ vinā pravasāmy aham
a evaṃ bruvāṇaṃ śatrughnaṃ pariṣvajyedam abravīt
c mā viṣādaṃ kṛthā vīra naitat kṣatriya ceṣṭitam
a nāvasīdanti rājāno vipravāseṣu rāghava
c prajāś ca paripālyā hi kṣatradharmeṇa rāghava
a kāle kāle ca māṃ vīra ayodhyām avalokitum
c āgaccha tvaṃ naraśreṣṭha gantāsi ca puraṃ tava
a mamāpi tvaṃ sudayitaḥ prāṇair api na saṃśayaḥ
c avaśyaṃ karaṇīyaṃ ca rājyasya paripālanam
a tasmāt tvaṃ vasa kākutstha pañcarātraṃ mayā saha
c ūrdhvaṃ gantāsi madhurāṃ sabhṛtyabalavāhanaḥ
a rāmasyaitad vacaḥ śrutvā dharmayuktaṃ mano'nugam
c śatrughno dīnayā vācā bāḍham ity eva cābravīt
a sa pañcarātraṃ kākutstho rāghavasya yathājñayā
c uṣya tatra maheṣvāso gamanāyopacakrame
a āmantrya tu mahātmānaṃ rāmaṃ satyaparākramam
c bharataṃ lakṣmaṇaṃ caiva mahāratham upāruhat
a dūraṃ tābhyām anugato lakṣmaṇena mahātmanā
c bharatena ca śatrughno jagāmāśu purīṃ tadā
a prasthāpya tu sa śatrughnaṃ bhrātṛbhyāṃ saha rāghavaḥ
c pramumoda sukhī rājyaṃ dharmeṇa paripālayan
a tataḥ katipayāhaḥsu vṛddho jānapado dvijaḥ
c śavaṃ bālam upādāya rājadvāram upāgamat
a rudan bahuvidhā vācaḥ snehākṣarasamanvitāḥ
c asakṛt putraputreti vākyam etad uvāca ha
a kiṃ nu me duṣkṛtaṃ karma pūrvaṃ dehāntare kṛtam
c yad ahaṃ putram ekaṃ tvāṃ paśyāmi nidhanaṃ gatam
a aprāptayauvanaṃ bālaṃ pañcavarṣasamanvitam
c akāle kālam āpannaṃ duḥkhāya mama putraka
a alpair ahobhir nidhanaṃ gamiṣyāmi na saṃśayaḥ
c ahaṃ ca jananī caiva tava śokena putraka
a na smarāmy anṛtaṃ hy uktaṃ na ca hiṃsāṃ smarāmy aham
c kena me duṣkṛtenādya bāla eva mamātmajaḥ
e akṛtvā pitṛkāryāṇi nīto vaivasvatakṣayam
a nedṛśaṃ dṛṣṭapūrvaṃ me śrutaṃ vā ghoradarśanam
c mṛtyur aprāptakālānāṃ rāmasya viṣaye yathā
a rāmasya duṣkṛtaṃ kiṃ cin mahad asti na saṃśayaḥ
c tvaṃ rājañ jīvayasvainaṃ bālaṃ mṛtyuvaśaṃ gatam
a bhrātṛbhiḥ sahito rājan dīrgham āyur avāpnuhi
c uṣitāḥ sma sukhaṃ rājye tavāsmin sumahābala
a saṃpraty anātho viṣaya ikṣvākūṇāṃ mahātmanām
c rāmaṃ nātham ihāsādya bālāntakaraṇaṃ nṛpam
a rājadoṣair vipadyante prajā hy avidhipālitāḥ
c asadvṛtte tu nṛpatāv akāle mriyate janaḥ
a yadā pureṣv ayuktāni janā janapadeśu ca
c kurvate na ca rakṣāsti tadākālakṛtaṃ bhayam
a savyaktaṃ rājadoṣo 'yaṃ bhaviṣyati na saṃśayaḥ
c pure janapade vāpi tadā bālavadho hy ayam
a evaṃ bahuvidhair vākyair nindayāno muhur muhuḥ
c rājānaṃ duḥkhasaṃtaptaḥ sutaṃ tam upagūhati
a tathā tu karuṇaṃ tasya dvijasya paridevitam
c śuśrāva rāghavaḥ sarvaṃ duḥkhaśokasamanvitam
a sa duḥkhena susaṃtapto mantriṇaḥ samupāhvayat
c vasiṣṭhaṃ vāmadevaṃ ca bhrātṝṃś ca sahanaigamān
a tato dvijā vasiṣṭhena sārdham aṣṭau praveśitāḥ
c rājānaṃ devasaṃkāśaṃ vardhasveti tato 'bruvan
a mārkaṇḍeyo 'tha maudgalyo vāmadevaś ca kāśyapaḥ
c kātyāyano 'tha jābālir gautamo nāradas tathā
a ete dvijarṣabhāḥ sarve āganeṣūpaveśitāḥ
c mantriṇo naigamāś caiva yathārham anukūlataḥ
a teṣāṃ samupaviṣṭānāṃ sarveṣāṃ dīptatejasām
c raghavaḥ sarvam ācaṣṭe dvijo yasmāt praroditi
a tasya tadvacanaṃ śrutvā rājño dīnasya nāradaḥ
c pratyuvāca śubhaṃ vākyam ṛṣīṇāṃ saṃnidhau nṛpam
a śṛṇu rājan yathākāle prāpto 'yaṃ bālasaṃkṣayaḥ
c śrutvā kartavyatāṃ vīra kuruṣva raghunandana
a purā kṛtayuge rāma brāhmaṇā vai tapasvinaḥ
c abrāhmaṇas tadā rājan na tapasvī kathaṃ cana
a tasmin yuge prajvalite brahmabhūte anāvṛte
c amṛtyavas tadā sarve jajñire dīrghadarśinaḥ
a tatas tretāyugaṃ nāma mānavānāṃ vapuṣmatām
c kṣatriyā yatra jāyante pūrveṇa tapasānvitāḥ
a vīryeṇa tapasā caiva te 'dhikāḥ pūrvajanmani
c mānavā ye mahātmānas tasmiṃs tretāyuge yuge
a brahmakṣatraṃ tu tat sarvaṃ yat pūrvam aparaṃ ca yat
c yugayor ubhayor āsīt samavīryasamanvitam
a apaśyantas tu te sarve viśeṣam adhikaṃ tataḥ
c sthāpanaṃ cakrire tatra cāturvarṇyasya sarvataḥ
a adharmaḥ pādam ekaṃ tu pātayat pṛthivītale
c adharmeṇa hi saṃyuktās tena mandābhavan dvijāḥ
a tataḥ prāduṣkṛtaṃ pūrvam āyuṣaḥ pariniṣṭhitam
c śubhāny evācaraṃl lokāḥ satyadharmaparāyaṇāḥ
a tretāyuge tv avartanta brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyaś ca ye
c tapo 'tapyanta te sarve śuśrūṣām apare janāḥ
a sa dharmaḥ paramas teṣāṃ vaiśyaśūdram athāgamat
c pūjāṃ ca sarvavarṇānāṃ śūdrāś cakrur viśeṣataḥ
a tataḥ pādam adharmasya dvitīyam avatārayat
c tato dvāparasaṃkhyā sā yugasya samajāyata
a tasmin dvāparasaṃkhye tu vartamāne yugakṣaye
c adharmaś cānṛtaṃ caiva vavṛdhe puruṣarṣabha
a tasmin dvāparasaṃkhyāte tapo vaiśyān samāviśat
c na śūdro labhate dharmam ugraṃ taptaṃ nararṣabha
a hīnavarṇo naraśreṣṭha tapyate sumahat tapaḥ
c bhaviṣyā śūdrayonyāṃ hi tapaścaryā kalau yuge
a adharmaḥ paramo rāma dvāpare śūdradhāritaḥ
c sa vai viṣayaparyante tava rājan mahātapāḥ
e śūdras tapyati durbuddhis tena bālavadho hy ayam
a yo hy adharmam akāryaṃ vā viṣaye pārthivasya hi
c karoti rājaśārdūla pure vā durmatir naraḥ
e kṣipraṃ hi narakaṃ yāti sa ca rājā na saṃśayaḥ
a sa tvaṃ puruṣaśārdūla mārgasva viṣayaṃ svakam
c duṣkṛtaṃ yatra paśyethās tatra yatnaṃ samācara
a evaṃ te dharmavṛddhiś ca nṛṇāṃ cāyurvivardhanam
c bhaviṣyati naraśreṣṭha bālasyāsya ca jīvitam
a nāradasya tu tad vākyaṃ śrutvāmṛtamayaṃ yathā
c praharṣam atulaṃ lebhe lakṣmaṇaṃ cedam abravīt
a gaccha saumya dvijaśreṣṭhaṃ samāśvāsaya lakṣmaṇa
c bālasya ca śarīraṃ tat tailadroṇyāṃ nidhāpaya
a gandhaiś ca paramodārais tailaiś ca susugandhibhiḥ
c yathā na kṣīyate bālas tathā saumya vidhīyatām
a yathā śarīre bālasya guptasyākliṣṭakarmaṇaḥ
c vipattiḥ paribhedo vā bhaven na ca tathā kuru
a tathā saṃdiśya kākutstho lakṣmaṇaṃ śubhalakṣaṇam
c manasā puṣpakaṃ dadhyāv āgaccheti mahāyaśāḥ
a iṅgitaṃ sa tu vijñāya puṣpako hemabhūṣitaḥ
c ājagāma muhūrtena saṃpīpaṃ rāghavasya vai
a so 'bravīt praṇato bhūtvā ayam asmi narādhipa
c vaśyas tava mahābāho kiṃkaraḥ samupasthitaḥ
a bhāṣitaṃ ruciraṃ śrutvā puṣpakasya narādhipaḥ
c abhivādya maharṣīs tān vimānaṃ so 'dhyarohata
a dhanur gṛhītvā tūṇīṃ ca khagdaṃ ca ruciraprabham
c nikṣipya nagare vīrau saumitribharatāv ubhau
a prāyāt pratīcīṃ sa marūn vicinvaṃś ca samantataḥ
c uttarām agamac chrīmān diśaṃ himavadāvṛtam
a apaśyamānas tatrāpi svalpam apy atha duṣkṛtam
c pūrvām api diśaṃ sarvām athāpaśyan narādhipaḥ
a dakṣiṇāṃ diśam ākrāmat tato rājarṣinandanaḥ
c śaivalasyottare pārśve dadarśa sumahat saraḥ
a tasmin sarasi tapyantaṃ tāpasaṃ sumahat tapaḥ
c dadarśa rāghavaḥ śrīmāṃl lambamānam adho mukham
a athainaṃ samupāgamya tapyantaṃ tapa uttamam
c uvāca rāghavo vākyaṃ dhanyas tvam asi suvrata
a kasyāṃ yonyāṃ tapovṛddhavartase dṛḍhavikrama
c kautūhalāt tvāṃ pṛcchāmi rāmo dāśarathir hy aham
a manīṣitas te ko nv arthaḥ svargalābho varāśrayaḥ
c yam aśritya tapas taptaṃ śrotum icchāmi tāpasa
a brāhmaṇo vāsi bhadraṃ te kṣatriyo vāsi durjayaḥ
c vaiśyo vā yadi vā śūdraḥ satyam etad bravīhi me
a tasya tadvacanaṃ śrutvā rāmasyākliṣṭakarmaṇaḥ
c avākśirās tathābhūto vākyam etad uvāca ha
a śūdrayonyāṃ prasūto 'smi tapa ugraṃ samāsthitaḥ
c devatvaṃ prārthaye rāma saśarīro mahāyaśaḥ
a na mithyāhaṃ vade rājan devalokajigīṣayā
c śūdraṃ māṃ viddhi kākutstha śambūkaṃ nāma nāmataḥ
a bhāṣatas tasya śūdrasya khaḍgaṃ suruciraprabham
c niṣkṛṣya kośād vimalaṃ śiraś ciccheda rāghavaḥ
a tasmin muhūrte bālo 'sau jīvena samayujyata
a tato 'gastyāśramapadaṃ rāmaḥ kamalalocanaḥ
c sa gatvā vinayenaiva taṃ natvā mumude sukhī
a so 'bhivādya mahātmānaṃ jvalantam iva tejasā
c ātithyaṃ paramaṃ prāpya niṣasāda narādhipaḥ
a tam uvāca mahātejāḥ kumbhayonir mahātapāḥ
c svāgataṃ te naraśreṣṭha diṣṭyā prāpto 'si rāghava
a tvaṃ me bahumato rāma guṇair bahubhir uttamaiḥ
c atithiḥ pūjanīyaś ca māma rājan hṛdi sthitaḥ
a surā hi kathayanti tvām āgataṃ śūdraghātinam
c brāhmaṇasya tu dharmeṇa tvayā jīvāpitaḥ sutaḥ
a uṣyatāṃ ceha rajanīṃ sakāśe mama rāghava
c prabhāte puṣpakeṇa tvaṃ gantā svapuram eva hi
a idaṃ cābharaṇaṃ saumya nirmitaṃ viśvakarmaṇā
c divyaṃ divyena vapuṣā dīpyamānaṃ svatejasā
e pratigṛhṇīṣva kākutstha matpriyaṃ kuru rāghava
a dattasya hi punar dānaṃ sumahat phalam ucyate
c tasmāt pradāsye vidhivat tat pratīccha nararṣabha
a tad rāmaḥ pratijagrāha munes tasya mahātmanaḥ
c divyam ābharaṇaṃ citraṃ pradīptam iva bhāskaram
a pratigṛhya tato rāmas tad ābharaṇam uttamam
c āgamaṃ tasya divyasya praṣṭum evopacakrame
a atyadbhutam idaṃ brahman vapuṣā yuktam uttamam
c kathaṃ bhagavatā prāptaṃ kuto vā kena vāhṛtam
a kutūhalatayā brahman pṛcchāmi tvāṃ mahāyaśaḥ
c āścaryāṇāṃ bahūnāṃ hi nidhiḥ paramako bhavān
a evaṃ bruvati kākutsthe munir vākyam athābravīt
c śṛṇu rāma yathāvṛttaṃ purā tretāyuge gate
a purā tretāyuge hy āsīd araṇyaṃ bahuvistaram
c samantād yojanaśataṃ nirmṛgaṃ pakṣivarjitam
a tasmin nirmānuṣe 'raṇye kurvāṇas tapa uttamam
c aham ākramituṃ śaumya tad araṇyam upāgamam
a tasya rūpam araṇyasya nirdeṣṭuṃ na śaśāka ha
c phalamūlaiḥ sukhāsvādair bahurūpaiś ca pādapaiḥ
a tasyāraṇyasya madhye tu saro yojanam āyatam
c padmotpalasamākīrṇaṃ samatikrāntaśaivalam
a tad āścaryam ivātyarthaṃ sukhāsvādam anuttamam
c arajaskaṃ tathākṣobhyaṃ śrīmatpakṣigaṇāyutam
a tasmin saraḥsamīpe tu mahad adbhutam āśramam
c purāṇaṃ puṇyam atyarthaṃ tapasvijanavarjitam
a tatrāham avasaṃ rātriṃ naidāghīṃ puruṣarṣabha
c prabhāte kālyam utthāya saras tad upacakrame
a athāpaśyaṃḥ śavaṃ tatra supuṣṭam ajaraṃ kva cit
c tiṣṭhantaṃ parayā lakṣmyā tasmiṃs toyāśaye nṛpa
a tam arthaṃ cintayāno 'haṃ muhūrtaṃ tatra rāghava
c viṣṭhito 'smi sarastīre kiṃ nv idaṃ syād iti prabho
a athāpaśyaṃ muhūrtāt tu divyam adbhutadarśanam
c vimānaṃ paramodāraṃ haṃsayuktaṃ manojavam
a atyarthaṃ svargiṇaṃ tatra vimāne raghunandana
c upāste 'psarasāṃ vīra sahasraṃ divyabhūṣaṇam
e gānti geyāni ramyāṇi vādayanti tathāparāḥ
a paśyato me tadā rāma vimānād avaruhya ca
c taṃ śavaṃ bhakṣayām āsa sa svargī raghunandana
a tato bhuktvā yathākāmaṃ māṃsaṃ bahu ca suṣṭhu ca
c avatīrya saraḥ svargī saṃspraṣṭum upacakrame
a upaspṛśya yathānyāyaṃ sa svargī puruṣarṣabha
c āroḍhum upacakrāma vimānavaram uttamam
a tam ahaṃ devasaṃkāśam ārohantam udīkṣya vai
c athāham abruvaṃ vākyaṃ tam eva puruṣarṣabha
a ko bhavān devasaṃkāśa āhāraś ca vigarhitaḥ
c tvayāyaṃ bhujyate saumya kiṃ karthaṃ vaktum arhasi
a āścaryam īdṛśo bhāvo bhāsvaro devasaṃmataḥ
c āhāro garhitaḥ saumya śrotum icchāmi tattvataḥ
a bhuktvā tu bhāṣitaṃ vākyaṃ mama rāma śubhākṣaram
c prāñjaliḥ pratyuvācedaṃ sa svargī raghunandana
a śṛṇu brahman yathāvṛttaṃ mamaitat sukhaduḥkhayoḥ
c duratikramaṇīyaṃ hi yathā pṛcchasi māṃ dvija
a purā vaidarbhako rājā pitā mama mahāyaśāḥ
c sudeva iti vikhyātas triṣu lokeṣu vīryavān
a tasya putradvayaṃ brahman dvābhyāṃ strībhyām ajāyata
c ahaṃ śveta iti khyāto yavīyān suratho 'bhavat
a tataḥ pitari svaryāte paurā mām abhyaṣecayan
c tatrāhaṃ kṛtavān rājyaṃ dharmeṇa susamāhitaḥ
a evaṃ varṣasahasrāṇi samatītāni suvrata
c rājyaṃ kārayato brahman prajā dharmeṇa rakṣataḥ
a so 'haṃ nimitte kasmiṃś cid vijñātāyur dvijottama
c kāladharmaṃ hṛdi nyasya tato vanam upāgamam
a so 'haṃ vanam idaṃ durgaṃ mṛgapakṣivivarjitam
c tapaś cartuṃ praviṣṭo 'smi samīpe sarasaḥ śubhe
a bhrātaraṃ surathaṃ rājye abhiṣicya narādhipam
c idaṃ saraḥ samāsādya tapas taptaṃ mayā ciram
a so 'haṃ varṣasahasrāṇi tapas trīṇi mahāmune
c taptvā suduṣkaraṃ prāpto brahmalokam anuttamam
a tato māṃ svargasaṃsthaṃ vai kṣutpipāse dvijottama
c bādhete paramodāra tato 'haṃ vyathitendriyaḥ
a gatvā tribhuvaṇaśreṣṭhaṃ pitāmaham uvāca ha
c bhagavan brahmaloko 'yaṃ kṣutpipāsāvivarjitaḥ
a kasyeyaṃ karmaṇaḥ prāptiḥ kṣutpipāsāvaśo 'smi yat
c āhāraḥ kaś ca me deva tan me brūhi pitāmaha
a pitāmahas tu mām āha tavāhāraḥ sudevaja
c svādūni svāni māṃsāni tāni bhakṣaya nityaśaḥ
a svaśarīraṃ tvayā puṣṭaṃ kurvatā tapa uttamam
c anuptaṃ rohate śveta na kadā cin mahāmate
a dattaṃ na te 'sti sūkṣmo 'pi vane sattvaniṣevite
c tena svargagato vatsa bādhyase kṣutpipāsayā
a sa tvaṃ supuṣṭam āhāraiḥ svaśarīram anuttamam
c bhakṣayasvāmṛtarasaṃ sā te tṛptir bhaviṣyati
a yadā tu tad vanaṃ śveta agastyaḥ sumahān ṛṣiḥ
c ākramiṣyati durdharṣas tadā kṛcchād vimokṣyase
a sa hi tārayituṃ saumya śaktaḥ suragaṇān api
c kiṃ punas tvāṃ mahābāho kṣutpipāsāvaśaṃ gatam
a so 'haṃ bhagavataḥ śrutvā devadevasya niścayam
c āhāraṃ garhitaṃ kurmi svaśarīraṃ dvijottama
a bahūn varṣagaṇān brahman bhujyamānam idaṃ mayā
c kṣayaṃ nābhyeti brahmarṣe tṛptiś cāpi mamottamā
a tasya me kṛcchrabhūtasya kṛcchrād asmād vimokṣaya
c anyeṣām agatir hy atra kumbhayonim ṛte dvijam
a idam ābharaṇaṃ saumya tāraṇārthaṃ dvijottama
c pratigṛhṇīṣva brahmarṣe prasādaṃ kartum arhasi
a tasyāhaṃ svargiṇo vākyaṃ śrutvā duḥkhasamanvitam
c tāraṇāyopajagrāha tad ābharaṇam uttamam
a mayā pratigṛhīte tu tasminn ābharaṇe śubhe
c mānuṣaḥ pūrvako deho rājarṣeḥ sa nanāśa ha
a pranaṣṭe tu śarīre 'sau rājarṣiḥ parayā mudā
c tṛptaḥ pramudito rājā jagāma tridivaṃ punaḥ
a tenedaṃ śakratulyena divyam ābharaṇaṃ mama
c tasmin nimitte kākutstha dattam adbhutadarśanam
a tad adbhutatamaṃ vākyaṃ śrutvāgastyasya rāghavaḥ
c gauravād vismayāc caiva bhūyaḥ praṣṭuṃ pracakrame
a bhagavaṃs tad vanaṃ ghoraṃ tapas tapyati yatra saḥ
c śveto vaidarbhako rājā kathaṃ tad amṛgadvijam
a niḥsattvaṃ ca vanaṃ jātaṃ śūnyaṃ manujavarjitam
c tapaś cartuṃ praviṣṭaḥ sa śrotum icchāmi tattvataḥ
a rāmasya bhāṣitaṃ śrutvā kautūhalasamanvitam
c vākyaṃ paramatejasvī vaktum evopacakrame
a purā kṛtayuge rāma manur daṇḍadharaḥ prabhuḥ
c tasya putro mahān āsīd ikṣvākuḥ kulavardhanaḥ
a taṃ putraṃ pūrvake rājye nikṣipya bhuvi durjayam
c pṛthivyāṃ rājavaṃśānāṃ bhava kartety uvāca ha
a tatheti ca pratijñātaṃ pituḥ putreṇa rāghava
c tataḥ paramasaṃhṛṣṭo manuḥ punar uvāca ha
a prīto 'smi paramodārakartā cāsi na saṃśayaḥ
c daṇḍena ca prajā rakṣa mā ca daṇḍam akāraṇe
a aparādhiṣu yo daṇḍaḥ pātyate mānaveṣu vai
c sa daṇḍo vidhivan muktaḥ svargaṃ nayati pārthivam
a tasmād daṇḍe mahābāho yatnavān bhava putraka
c dharmo hi paramo loke kurvatas te bhaviṣyati
a iti taṃ bahu saṃdiśya manuḥ putraṃ samādhinā
c jagāma tridivaṃ hṛṣṭo brahmalokam anuttamam
a prayāte tridive tasminn ikṣvākur amitaprabhaḥ
c janayiṣye kathaṃ putrān iti cintāparo 'bhavat
a karmabhir bahurūpaiś ca tais tair manusutaḥ sutān
c janayām āsa dharmātmā śataṃ devasutopamān
a teṣām avarajas tāta sarveṣāṃ raghunandana
c mūḍhaś cākṛtividyaś ca na śuśrūṣati pūrvajān
a nāma tasya ca daṇḍeti pitā cakre 'lpatejasaḥ
c avaśyaṃ daṇḍapatanaṃ śarīre 'sya bhaviṣyati
a sa paśyamānas taṃ doṣaṃ ghoraṃ putrasya rāghava
c vindhyaśaivalayor madhye rājyaṃ prādād ariṃdama
a sa daṇḍas tatra rājābhūd ramye parvatarodhasi
c puraṃ cāpratimaṃ rāma nyaveśayad anuttamam
a purasya cākaron nāma madhumantam iti prabho
c purohitaṃ cośanasaṃ varayām āsa suvratam
a evaṃ sa rājā tad rājyaṃ kārayat sapurohitaḥ
c prahṛṣṭamanujākīrṇaṃ devarājyaṃ yathā divi
a etad ākhyāya rāmāya maharṣiḥ kumbhasaṃbhavaḥ
c asyām evāparaṃ vākyaṃ kathāyām upacakrame
a tataḥ sa daṇḍaḥ kākutstha bahuvarṣagaṇāyutam
c akarot tatra mandātmā rājyaṃ nihatakaṇṭakam
a atha kāle tu kasmiṃś cid rājā bhārgavam āśramam
c ramaṇīyam upākrāmac caitre māsi manorame
a tatra bhārgavakanyāṃ sa rūpeṇāpratimāṃ bhuvi
c vicarantīṃ vanoddeśe daṇḍo 'paśyad anuttamām
a sa dṛṣṭvā tāṃ sudurmedhā anaṅgaśarapīḍitaḥ
c abhigamya susaṃvignaḥ kanyāṃ vacanam abravīt
a kutas tvam asi suśroṇi kasya vāsi sutā śubhe
c pīḍito 'ham anaṅgena pṛcchāmi tvāṃ sumadhyame
a tasya tv evaṃ bruvāṇasya mohonmattasya kāminaḥ
c bhārgavī pratyuvācedaṃ vacaḥ sānunayaṃ nṛpam
a bhārgavasya sutāṃ viddhi devasyākliṣṭakarmaṇaḥ
c arajāṃ nāma rājendra jyeṣṭhām āśramavāsinīm
a guruḥ pitā me rājendra tvaṃ ca śiṣyo mahātmanaḥ
c vyasanaṃ sumahat kruddhaḥ sa te dadyān mahātapāḥ
a yadi vātra mayā kāryaṃ dharmadṛṣṭena satpathā
c varayasva nṛpa śreṣṭha pitaraṃ me mahādyutim
a anyathā tu phalaṃ tubhyaṃ bhaved ghorābhisaṃhitam
c krodhena hi pitā me 'sau trailokyam api nirdahet
a evaṃ bruvāṇām arajāṃ daṇḍaḥ kāmaśarārditaḥ
c pratyuvāca madonmattaḥ śirasy ādhāya so 'ñjalim
a prasādaṃ kuru suśroṇi na kālaṃ kṣeptum arhasi
c tvatkṛte hi mama prāṇā vidīryante śubhānane
a tvāṃ prāpya hi vadho vāpi pāpaṃ vāpi sudāruṇam
c bhaktaṃ bhajasva māṃ bhīru bhajamānaṃ suvihvalam
a evam uktvā tu tāṃ kanyāṃ dorbhyāṃ gṛhya balād balī
c visphurantīṃ yathākāmaṃ maithunāyopacakrame
a tam anarthaṃ mahāghoraṃ daṇḍaḥ kṛtvā sudāruṇam
c nagaraṃ prayayau cāśu madhumantam anuttamam
a arajāpi rudantī sā āśramasyāvidūrataḥ
c pratīkṣate susaṃtrastā pitaraṃ devasaṃnibham
a sa muhūrtād upaśrutya devarṣir amitaprabhaḥ
c svam āśramaṃ śiṣya vṛtaḥ kṣudhārtaḥ saṃnyavartata
a so 'paśyad arajāṃ dīnāṃ rajasā samabhiplutām
c jyotsnām ivāruṇagrastāṃ pratyūṣe na virājatīm
a tasya roṣaḥ samabhavat kṣudhārtasya viśeṣataḥ
c nirdahann iva lokāṃs trīñ śiṣyāṃś cedam uvāca ha
a paśyadhvaṃ viparītasya daṇḍasyāviditātmanaḥ
c vipattiṃ ghorasaṃkāśāṃ kruddhām agniśikhām iva
a kṣayo 'sya durmateḥ prāptaḥ sānugasya durātmanaḥ
c yaḥ pradīptāṃ hutāśasya śikhāṃ vai spraṣṭum icchati
a yasmāt sa kṛtavān pāpam īdṛśaṃ ghoradarśanam
c tasmāt prāpsyati durmedhāḥ phalaṃ pāpasya karmaṇaḥ
a saptarātreṇa rājāsau sabhṛtyabalavāhanaḥ
c pāpakarmasamācāro vadhaṃ prāpsyati durmatiḥ
a samantād yojanaśataṃ viṣayaṃ cāsya durmateḥ
c dhakṣyate pāṃsuvarṣeṇa mahatā pākaśāsanaḥ
a sarvasattvāni yānīha sthāvarāṇi carāṇi ca
c mahatā pāṃsuvarṣeṇa nāśaṃ yāsyanti sarvaśaḥ
a daṇḍasya viṣayo yāvat tāvat sarvasamucchrayaḥ
c pāṃsubhuta ivālakṣyaḥ saptarātrād bhaviṣyati
a ity uktvā krodhasaṃtapas tam āśramanivāsinam
c janaṃ janapadānteṣu sthīyatām iti cābravīt
a śrutvā tūśasano vākyaṃ sa āśramāvasatho janaḥ
c niṣkrānto viṣayāt tasya sthānaṃ cakre 'tha bāhyataḥ
a sa tathoktvā munijanam arajām idam abravīt
c ihaiva vasa durmedhe āśrame susamāhitā
a idaṃ yojanaparyantaṃ saraḥ suruciraprabham
c araje vijvarā bhuṅkṣva kālaś cātra pratīkṣyatām
a tvatsamīpe tu ye sattvā vāsam eṣyanti tāṃ niśām
c avadhyāḥ pāṃsuvarṣeṇa te bhaviṣyanti nityadā
a ity uktvā bhārgavo vāsam anyatra samupākramat
c saptāhād bhasmasādbhūtaṃ yathoktaṃ brahmavādinā
a tasyāsau daṇḍaviṣayo vindhyaśaivalasānuṣu
c śapto brahmarṣiṇā tena purā vaidharmake kṛte
a tataḥ prabhṛti kākutstha daṇḍakāraṇyam ucyate
c tapasvinaḥ sthitā yatra janasthānam atho 'bhavat
a etat te sarvam ākhyātaṃ yan māṃ pṛcchasi rāghava
c saṃdhyām upāsituṃ vīra samayo hy ativartate
a ete maharṣayaḥ sarve pūrṇakumbhāḥ samantataḥ
c kṛtodako naravyāghra ādityaṃ paryupāsate
a sa tair ṛṣibhir abhyastaḥ sahitair brahmasattamaiḥ
c ravir astaṃ gato rāma gacchodakam upaspṛśa
a ṛṣer vacanam ājñāya rāmaḥ saṃdhyām upāsitum
c upākrāmat saraḥ puṇyam apsarobhir niṣevitam
a tatrodakam upaspṛṣśya saṃdhyām anvāsya paścimām
c āśramaṃ prāviśad rāmaḥ kumbhayoner mahātmanaḥ
a asyāgastyo bahuguṇaṃ phalamūlaṃ tathauṣadhīḥ
c śākāni ca pavitrāṇi bhojanārtham akalpayat
a sa bhuktavān naraśreṣṭhas tad annam amṛtopamam
c prītaś ca parituṣṭaś ca tāṃ rātriṃ samupāvasat
a prabhāte kālyam utthāya kṛtvāhnikam ariṃdamaḥ
c ṛṣiṃ samabhicakrāma gamanāya raghūttamaḥ
a abhivādyābravīd rāmo maharṣiṃ kumbhasaṃbhavam
c āpṛcche tvāṃ gamiṣyāmi mām anujñātum arhasi
a dhanyo 'smy anugṛhīto 'smi darśanena mahātmanaḥ
c draṣṭuṃ caivāgamiṣyāmi pāvanārtham ihātmanaḥ
a tathā vadati kākutsthe vākyam adbhutadarśanam
c uvāca paramaprīto dharmanetras tapodhanaḥ
a atyadbhutam idaṃ vākyaṃ tava rāma śubhākṣaram
c pāvanaḥ sarvalokānāṃ tvam eva raghunandana
a muhūrtam api rāma tvāṃ ye nu paśyanti ke cana
c pāvitāḥ svargabhūtās te pūjyante divi daivataiḥ
a ye ca tvāṃ ghoracakṣurbhir īkṣante prāṇino bhuvi
c hatās te yamadaṇḍena sadyo nirayagāminaḥ
a gaccha cāriṣṭam avyagraḥ panthānam akutobhayam
c praśādhi rājyaṃ dharmeṇa gatir hi jagato bhavān
a evam uktas tu muninā prāñjaliḥ prpagraho nṛpaḥ
c abhyavādayata prājñas tam ṛṣiṃ puṇyaśīlinam
a abhivādya muniśreṣṭhaṃ tāṃś ca sarvāṃs tapodhanān
c adhyārohat tad avyagraḥ puṣpakaṃ hemabhūṣitam
a taṃ prayāntaṃ munigaṇā āśīrvādaiḥ samantataḥ
c apūjayan mahendrābhaṃ sahasrākṣam ivāmarāḥ
a svasthaḥ sa dadṛśe rāmaḥ puṣpake hemabhūṣite
c śaśī meghasamīpastho yathā jaladharāgame
a tato 'rdhadivase prāpte pūjyamānas tatas tataḥ
c ayodhyāṃ prāpya kākutstho vimānād avarohata
a tato visṛjya ruciraṃ puṣpakaṃ kāmagāminam
c kakṣyāntaravinikṣiptaṃ dvāḥsthaṃ rāmo 'bravīd vacaḥ
a lakṣmaṇaṃ bharataṃ caiva gatvā tau laghuvikramau
c mamāgamanam ākhyāya śabdāpaya ca māṃ ciram
a tac chrutvā bhāṣitaṃ tasya rāmasyākliṣṭakarmaṇaḥ
c dvāḥsthaḥ kumārāv āhūya rāghavāya nyavedayat
a dṛṣṭvā tu rāghavaḥ prāptau priyau bharatalakṣmaṇau
c pariṣvajya tato rāmo vākyam etad uvāca ha
a kṛtaṃ mayā yathātathyaṃ dvijakāryam anuttamam
c dharmasetumato bhūyaḥ kartum icchāmi rāghavau
a yuvābhyām ātmabhūtābhyāṃ rājasūyam anuttamam
c sahito yaṣṭum icchāmi tatra dharmo hi śāśvataḥ
a iṣṭvā tu rājasūyena mitraḥ śatrunibarhaṇaḥ
c suhutena suyajñena varuṇatvam upāgamat
a somaś ca rājasūyena iṣṭvā dharmeṇa dharmavit
c prāptaś ca sarvalokānāṃ kīrtiṃ sthānaṃ ca śāśvatam
a asminn ahani yac chreyaś cintyatāṃ tan mayā saha
c hitaṃ cāyati yuktaṃ ca prayatau vaktum arhatha
a śrutā tu rāghavasyaitad vākyaṃ vākyaviśāradaḥ
c bharataḥ prāñjalir bhūtvā vākyam etad uvāca ha
a tvayi dharmaḥ paraḥ sādho tvayi sarvā vasuṃdharā
c pratiṣṭhitā mahābāho yaśaś cāmitavikrama
a mahīpālāś ca sarve tvāṃ prajāpatim ivāmarāḥ
c nirīkṣante mahātmāno lokanāthaṃ yathā vayam
a prajāś ca pitṛvad rājan paśyanti tvāṃ mahābala
c pṛthivyāṃ gatibhūto 'si prāṇinām api rāghava
a sa tvam evaṃvidhaṃ yajñam āhartāsi kathaṃ nṛpa
c pṛthivyāṃ rājavaṃśānāṃ vināśo yatra dṛśyate
a pṛthivyāṃ ye ca puruṣā rājan pauruṣam āgatāḥ
c sarveṣāṃ bhavitā tatra kṣayaḥ sarvāntakopamaḥ
a sa tvaṃ puruṣaśārdūla guṇair atulavikrama
c pṛthivīṃ nārhase hantuṃ vaśe hi tava vartate
a bharatasya tu tad vākyaṃ śrutvāmṛtamayaṃ yathā
c praharṣam atulaṃ lebhe rāmaḥ satyaparākramaḥ
a uvāca ca śubhāṃ vāṇīṃ kaikeyyā nandivardhanam
c prīto 'smi parituṣṭo 'smi tavādya vacanena hi
a idaṃ vacanam aklībaṃ tvayā dharmasamāhitam
c vyāhṛtaṃ puruṣavyāghra pṛthivyāḥ paripālanam
a eṣa tasmād abhiprāyād rājasūyāt kratūttamān
c nivartayāmi dharmajña tava suvyāhṛtena vai
a prajānāṃ pālanaṃ dharmo rājñāṃ yajñena saṃmitaḥ
c tasmāc chṛṇomi te vākyaṃ sādhūktaṃ susamāhitam
a tathoktavati rāme tu bharate ca mahātmani
c lakṣmaṇo 'pi śubhaṃ vākyam uvāca raghunandanam
a aśvamedho mahāyajñaḥ pāvanaḥ sarvapāpmanām
c pāvanas tava durdharṣo rocatāṃ kratupuṃgavaḥ
a śrūyate hi purāvṛttaṃ vāsave sumahātmani
c brahmahatyāvṛtaḥ śakro hayamedhena pāvitaḥ
a purā kila mahābāho devāsurasamāgame
c vṛtro nāma mahān āsīd daiteyo lokasaṃmataḥ
a vistīrṇā yojanaśatam ucchritas triguṇaṃ tataḥ
c anurāgeṇa lokāṃs trīn snehāt paśyati sarvataḥ
a dharmajñaś ca kṛtajñaś ca buddhyā ca pariniṣṭhitaḥ
c śaśāsa pṛthivīṃ sarvāṃ dharmeṇa susamāhitaḥ
a tasmin praśāsati tadā sarvakāmadughā mahī
c rasavanti prasūtāni mūlāni ca phalāni ca
a akṛṣṭapacyā pṛthivī susaṃpannā mahātmanaḥ
c sa rājyaṃ tādṛśaṃ bhuṅkte sphītam adbhutadarśanam
a tasya buddhiḥ samutpannā tapaḥ kuryām anuttamam
c tapo hi paramaṃ śreyas tapo hi paramaṃ sukham
a sa nikṣipya sutaṃ jyeṣṭhaṃ paureṣu parameśvaram
c tapa ugram upātiṣṭhat tāpayan sarvadevatāḥ
a tapas tapyati vṛtre tu vāsavaḥ paramārtavat
c viṣṇuṃ samupasaṃkramya vākyam etad uvāca ha
a tapasyatā mahābāho lokā vṛtreṇa nirjitāḥ
c balavān sa hi dharmātmā nainaṃ śakṣyāmi bādhitum
a yady asau tapa ātiṣṭhed bhūya eva sureśvara
c yāval lokā dhariṣyanti tāvad asya vaśānugāḥ
a tvaṃ cainaṃ paramodāram upekṣasi mahābala
c kṣaṇaṃ hi na bhaved vṛtraḥ kruddhe tvayi sureśvara
a yadā hi prītisaṃyogaṃ tvayā viṣṇo samāgataḥ
c tadā prabhṛti lokānāṃ nāthatvam upalabdhavān
a sa tvaṃ prasādaṃ lokānāṃ kuruṣva sumahāyaśaḥ
c tvatkṛtena hi sarvaṃ syāt praśāntam ajaraṃ jagat
a ime hi sarve viṣṇo tvāṃ nirīkṣante divaukasaḥ
c vṛtraghatena mahatā eṣāṃ sāhyaṃ kuruṣva ha
a tvayā hi nityaśaḥ sāhyaṃ kṛtam eṣāṃ mahātmanām
c asahyam idam anyeṣām agatīnāṃ gatir bhavān
a lakṣmaṇasya tu tad vākyaṃ śrutvā śatrunibarhaṇaḥ
c vṛtraghātam aśeṣeṇa kathayety āha lakṣmaṇam
a rāghaveṇaivam uktas tu sumitrānandavardhanaḥ
c bhūya eva kathāṃ divyāṃ kathayām āsa lakṣmaṇaḥ
a sahasrākṣavacaḥ śrutvā sarveṣāṃ ca divaukasām
c viṣṇur devān uvācedaṃ sarvān indrapurogamān
a pūrvaṃ sauhṛdabaddho 'smi vṛtrasya sumahātmanaḥ
c tena yuṣmat priyārthaṃ vai nāhaṃ hanmi mahāsuram
a avaśyaṃ karaṇīyaṃ ca bhavatāṃ sukham uttamam
c tasmād upāyam ākhyāsye yena vṛtraṃ haniṣyatha
a tridhā bhūtaṃ kariṣye 'ham ātmānaṃ surasattamāḥ
c tena vṛtraṃ sahasrākṣo haniṣyati na saṃśayaḥ
a eko 'ṃśo vāsavaṃ yātu dvitīyo vajram eva tu
c tṛtīyo bhūtalaṃ śakras tato vṛtraṃ haniṣyati
a tathā bruvati deveśe devā vākyam athābruvan
c evam etan na saṃdeho yathā vadasi daityahan
a bhadraṃ te 'stu gamiṣyāmo vṛtrāsuravadhaiṣiṇaḥ
c bhajasva paramodāravāsavaṃ svena tejasā
a tataḥ sarve mahātmānaḥ sahasrākṣapurogamāḥ
c tad araṇyam upākrāman yatra vṛtro mahāsuraḥ
a te 'paśyaṃs tejasā bhūtaṃ tapantam asurottamam
c pibantam iva lokāṃs trīn nirdahantam ivāmbaram
a dṛṣṭvaiva cāsuraśreṣṭhaṃ devās trāsam upāgaman
c katham enaṃ vadhiṣyāmaḥ kathaṃ na syāt parājayaḥ
a teṣāṃ cintayatāṃ tatra sahasrākṣaḥ puraṃdaraḥ
c vajraṃ pragṛhya bāhubhyāṃ prahiṇod vṛtramūrdhani
a kālāgnineva ghoreṇa dīpteneva mahārciṣā
c prataptaṃ vṛtraśirasi jagat trāsam upāgamat
a asaṃbhāvyaṃ vadhaṃ tasya vṛtrasya vibudhādhipaḥ
c cintayāno jagāmāśu lokasyāntaṃ mahāyaśāḥ
a tam indraṃ brahmahatyāśu gacchantam anugacchati
c apatac cāsya gātreṣu tam indraṃ duḥkham āviśat
a hatārayaḥ pranaṣṭendrā devāḥ sāgnipurogamāḥ
c viṣṇuṃ tribhuvaṇaśreṣṭhaṃ muhur muhur apūjayan
a tvaṃ gatiḥ paramā deva pūrvajo jagataḥ prabhuḥ
c rathārthaṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ viṣṇutvam upajagmivān
a hataś cāyaṃ tvayā vṛtro brahmahatyā ca vāsavam
c bādhate suraśārdūla mokṣaṃ tasya vinirdiśa
a teṣāṃ tad vacanaṃ śrutvā devānāṃ viṣṇur abravīt
c mām eva yajatāṃ śakraḥ pāvayiṣyāmi vajriṇam
a puṇyena hayamedhena mām iṣṭvā pākaśāsanaḥ
c punar eṣyati devānām indratvam akutobhayaḥ
a evaṃ saṃdiśya devānāṃ tāṃ vāṇīm amṛtopamā
c jagāma viṣṇur deveśaḥ stūyamānas triviṣṭapam
a tathā vṛtravadhaṃ sarvam akhilena sa lakṣmaṇaḥ
c kathayitvā naraśreṣṭhaḥ kathāśeṣam upākramat
a tato hate mahāvīrye vṛtre devabhayaṃkare
c brahmahatyāvṛtaḥ śakraḥ saṃjñāṃ lebhe na vṛtrahā
a so 'ntam āśritya lokānāṃ naṣṭasaṃjño vicetanaḥ
c kālaṃ tatrāvasat kaṃ cid veṣṭamāno yathoragaḥ
a atha naṣṭe sahasrākṣe udvignam abhavaj jagat
c bhūmiś ca dhvastasaṃkāśā niḥsnehā śuṣkakānanā
a niḥsrotasaś cāmbuvāhā hradāś ca saritas tathā
c saṃkṣobhaś caiva sattvānām anāvṛṣṭikṛto 'bhavat
a kṣīyamāṇe tu loke 'smin saṃbhrāntamanasaḥ surāḥ
c yad uktaṃ viṣṇunā pūrvaṃ taṃ yajñaṃ samupānayan
a tataḥ sarve suragaṇāḥ sopādhyāyāḥ saharṣibhiḥ
c taṃ deśaṃ sahitā jagmur yatrendro bhayamohitaḥ
a te tu dṛṣṭvā sahasrākṣaṃ mohitaṃ brahmahatyayā
c taṃ puraskṛtya deveśam aśvamedhaṃ pracakrire
a tato 'śvamedhaḥ sumahān mahendrasya mahātmanaḥ
c vavṛdhe brahmahatyāyāḥ pāvanārthaṃ nareśvara
a tato yajñasamāptau tu brahmahatyā mahātmanaḥ
c abhigamyābravīd vākyaṃ kva me sthānaṃ vidhāsyatha
a te tām ūcus tato devās tuṣṭāḥ prītisamanvitāḥ
c caturdhā vibhajātmānam ātmanaiva durāsade
a devānāṃ bhāṣitaṃ śrutvā brahmahatyā mahātmanām
c saṃnidhau sthānam anyatra varayām āsa durvasā
a ekenāṃśena vatsyāmi pūrṇodāsu nadīṣu vai
c dvitīyena tu vṛkṣeṣu satyam etad bravīmi vaḥ
a yo 'yam aṃśas tṛtīyo me strīṣu yauvanaśāliṣu
c trirātraṃ darpaparṇāsu vasiṣye darpaghātinī
a hantāro brāhmaṇān ye tu prekṣāpūrvam adūṣakān
c tāṃś caturthena bhāgena saṃśrayiṣye surarṣabhāḥ
a pratyūcus tāṃ tato devā yathā vadasi durvase
c tathā bhavatu tat sarvaṃ sādhayasva yathepsitam
a tataḥ prītyānvitā devāḥ sahasrākṣaṃ vavandire
c vijvaraḥ pūtapāpmā ca vāsavaḥ samapadyata
a praśāntaṃ ca jagat sarvaṃ sahasrākṣe pratiṣṭhate
c yajñaṃ cādbhutasaṃkāśaṃ tadā śakro 'bhyapūjayat
a īdṛśo hy aśvamedhasya prabhāvo raghunandana
c yajasva sumahābhāga hayamedhena pārthiva
a tac chrutvā lakṣmaṇenoktaṃ vākyaṃ vākyaviśāradaḥ
c pratyuvāca mahātejāḥ prahasan rāghavo vacaḥ
a evam etan naraśreṣṭha yathā vadasi lakṣmaṇa
c vṛtraghātam aśeṣeṇa vājimedhaphalaṃ ca yat
a śrūyate hi purā saumya kardamasya prajāpateḥ
c putro bāhlīśvaraḥ śrīmān ilo nāma sudhārmikaḥ
a sa rājā pṛthivīṃ sarvāṃ vaśe kṛtvā mahāyaśāḥ
c rājyaṃ caiva naravyāghra putravat paryapālayat
a suraiś ca paramodārair daiteyaiś ca mahāsuraiḥ
c nāgarākṣasagandharvair yakṣaiś ca sumahātmabhiḥ
a pūjyate nityaśaḥ saumya bhayārtai raghunandana
c abibhyaṃś ca trayo lokāḥ saroṣasya mahātmanaḥ
a sa rājā tādṛśo hy āsīd dharme vīrye ca niṣṭhitaḥ
c buddhyā ca paramodāro bāhlīkānāṃ mahāyaśāḥ
a sa pracakre mahābāhur mṛgayāṃ rucire vane
c caitre manorame māsi sabhṛtyabalavāhanaḥ
a prajaghne sa nṛpo 'raṇye mṛgāñ śatasahasraśaḥ
c hatvaiva tṛptir nābhūc ca rājñas tasya mahātmanaḥ
a nānāmṛgāṇām ayutaṃ vadhyamānaṃ mahātmanā
c yatra jāto mahāsenas taṃ deśam upacakrame
a tasmiṃs tu devadeveśaḥ śailarājasutāṃ haraḥ
c ramayām āsa durdharṣaiḥ sarvair anucaraiḥ saha
a kṛtvā strībhūtam ātmānam umeśo gopatidhvajaḥ
c devyāḥ priyacikīrṣuḥ sa tasmin parvatanirjhare
a ye ca tatra vanoddeśe sattvāḥ puruṣavādinaḥ
c yac ca kiṃ cana tat sarvaṃ nārīsaṃjñaṃ babhūva ha
a etasminn antare rājā sa ilaḥ kardamātmajaḥ
c nighnan mṛgasahasrāṇi taṃ deśam upacakrame
a sa dṛṣṭvā strīkṛtaṃ sarvaṃ savyālamṛgapakṣiṇam
c ātmānaṃ sānugaṃ caiva strībhūtaṃ raghunandana
a tasya duḥkhaṃ mahat tv āsīd dṛṣṭvātmānaṃ tathā gatam
c umāpateś ca tat karma jñātvā trāsam upāgamat
a tato devaṃ mahātmānaṃ śitikaṇṭhaṃ kapardinam
c jagāma śaraṇaṃ rājā sabhṛtyabalavāhanaḥ
a tataḥ prahasya varadaḥ saha devyā mahāyaśāḥ
c prajāpatisutaṃ vākyam uvāca varadaḥ svayam
a uttiṣṭhottiṣṭha rājarṣe kārdameya mahābala
c puruṣatvam ṛte saumya varaṃ varaya suvrata
a tataḥ sa rājā śokārtāḥ pratyākhyāto mahātmanā
c na sa jagrāha strībhūto varam anyaṃ surottamāt
a tataḥ śokena mahatā śailarājasutāṃ nṛpaḥ
c praṇipatya mahādevīṃ sarveṇaivāntarātmanā
a īśe varāṇāṃ varade lokānām asi bhāmini
c amoghadarśane devi bhaje saumye namo 'stu te
a hṛdgataṃ tasya rājarṣer vijñāya harasaṃnidhau
c pratyuvāca śubhaṃ vākyaṃ devī rudrasya saṃmatā
a ardhasya devo varado varārdhasya tathā hy aham
c tasmād ardhaṃ gṛhāṇa tvaṃ strīpuṃsor yāvad icchasi
a tad adbhutatamaṃ śrutvā devyā varam anuttamam
c saṃprahṛṣṭamanā bhūtvā rājā vākyam athābravīt
a yadi devi prasannā me rūpeṇāpratimā bhuvi
c māsaṃ strītvam upāsitvā māsaṃ syāṃ puruṣaḥ punaḥ
a īpsitaṃ tasya vijñāya devī surucirānanā
c pratyuvāca śubhaṃ vākyam evam etad bhaviṣyati
a rājan puruṣabhūtas tvaṃ strībhāvaṃ na smariṣyasi
c strībhūtaś cāparaṃ māsaṃ na smariṣyasi pauruṣam
a evaṃ sa rājā puruṣo māmaṃ bhūtvātha kārdamiḥ
c trailokyasundarī nārī māsam ekam ilābhavat
a tāṃ kathām ilasaṃbaddhāṃ rāmeṇa samudīritām
c lakṣmaṇo bharataś caiva śrutvā paramavismitau
a tau rāmaṃ prāñjalībhūtvā tasya rājño mahātmanaḥ
c vistaraṃ tasya bhāvasya tadā papracchatuḥ punaḥ
a kathaṃ sa rājā strībhūto vartayām āsa durgatim
c puruṣo vā yadā bhūtaḥ kāṃ vṛttiṃ vartayaty asau
a tayos tad bhāṣitaṃ śrutvā kautūhalasamanvitam
c kathayām āsa kākutṣṭhas tasya rājño yathā gatam
a tam eva prathamaṃ māsaṃ strībhūtvā lokasundarī
c tābhiḥ parivṛtā strībhir ye 'sya pūrvaṃ padānugāḥ
a tat kānanaṃ vigāhyāśu vijahre lokasundarī
c drumagulmalatākīrṇaṃ padbhyāṃ padmadalekṣaṇā
a vāhanāni ca sarvāṇi saṃtyaktvā vai samantataḥ
c parvatābhogavivare tasmin reme ilā tadā
a atha tasmin vanoddeśe parvatasyāvidūrataḥ
c saraḥ suruciraprakhyaṃ nānāpakṣigaṇāyutam
a dadarśa sā ilā tasmin budhaṃ somasutaṃ tadā
c jvalantaṃ svena vapuṣā pūrṇaṃ somam ivoditam
a tapantaṃ ca tapas tīvram ambhomadhye durāsadam
c yaśak saraṃ kāmagamaṃ tāruṇye paryavasthitam
a sā taṃ jalāśayaṃ sarvaṃ kṣobhayām āsa vismitā
c saha taiḥ pūra puruṣaiḥ strībhūtai raghunandana
a budhas tu tāṃ nirīkṣyaiva kāmabāṇābhipīḍitaḥ
c nopalebhe tadātmānaṃ cacāla ca tadāmbhasi
a ilāṃ nirīkṣamāṇaḥ sa trailokyābhyadhikāṃ śubhām
c cintāṃ samabhyatikrāmat kā nv iyaṃ devatādhikā
a na devīṣu na nāgīṣu nāsurīṣv apsaraḥsu ca
c dṛṣṭapūrvā mayā kā cid rūpeṇaitena śobhitā
a sadṛśīyaṃ mama bhaved yadi nānyaparigrahā
c iti buddhiṃ samāsthāya jalāt sthalam upāgamat
a sa āśramaṃ samupāgamya catasraḥ pramadās tataḥ
c śabdāpayata dharmātmā tāś cainaṃ ca vavandire
a sa tāḥ papraccha dharmātma kasyaiṣā lokasundarī
c kimartham āgatā ceha satyam ākhyāta māciram
a śubhaṃ tu tasya tadvākyaṃ madhuraṃ madhurākṣaram
c śrutvā tu tāḥ striyaḥ sarvā ūcur madhurayā girā
a asmākam eṣā suśroṇī prabhutve vartate sadā
c apatiḥ kānanānteṣu sahāsmābhir aṭaty asau
a tad vākyam avyaktapadaṃ tāsāṃ strīṇāṃ niśamya tu
c vidyām āvartanīṃ puṇyām āvartayata sa dvijaḥ
a so 'rthaṃ viditvā nikhilaṃ tasya rājño yathāgatam
c sarvā eva striyas tāś ca babhāṣe munipuṃgavaḥ
a atra kiṃ puruṣā bhadrā avasañ śailarodhasi
c vatsyathāsmin girau yūyam avakāśo vidhīyatām
a mūlaputraphalaiḥ sarvā vartayiṣyatha nityadā
c striyaḥ kimpuruṣān nāma bhartṝn samupalapsyatha
a tāḥ śrutvā somaputrasya vācaṃ kiṃpuruṣīkṛtāḥ
c upāsāṃ cakrire śailaṃ bahvyas tā bahudhā tadā
a śrutvā kimpuruṣotpattiṃ lakṣmaṇo bharatas tadā
c āścaryam iti cābrūtām ubhau rāmaṃ janeśvaram
a atha rāmaḥ kathām etāṃ bhūya eva mahāyaśāḥ
c kathayām āsa dharmātmā prajāpatisutasya vai
a sarvās tā vidrutā dṛṣṭvā kiṃnarīr ṛṣisattamaḥ
c uvāca rūpasaṃpannāṃ tāṃ striyaṃ prahasann iva
a somasyāhaṃ sudayitaḥ sutaḥ surucirānane
c bhajasva māṃ varārohe bhaktyā snigdhena cakṣuṣā
a tasya tadvacanaṃ śrutvā śūnye svajanavarjitā
c ilā suruciraprakhyaṃ pratyuvāca mahāgraham
a ahaṃ kāmakarī saumya tavāsmi vaśavartinī
c praśādhi māṃ somasuta yathecchasi tathā kuru
a tasyās tad adbhutaprakhyaṃ śrutvā harṣasamanvitaḥ
c sa vai kāmī saha tayā reme candramasaḥ sutaḥ
a budhasya mādhavo māsas tām ilāṃ rucirānanām
c gato ramayato 'tyarthaṃ kṣaṇavat tasya kāminaḥ
a atha māse tu saṃpūrṇe pūrṇendusadṛśānanaḥ
c prajāpatisutaḥ śrīmāñ śayane pratyabudhyata
a so 'paśyat somajaṃ tatra tapyantaṃ salilāśaye
c ūrdhvabāhuṃ nirālambaṃ taṃ rājā pratyabhāṣata
a bhagavan parvataṃ durgaṃ praviṣṭo 'smi sahānugaḥ
c na ca paśyāmi tat sainyaṃ kva nu te māmakā gatāḥ
a tac chrutvā tasya rājarṣer naṣṭasaṃjñasya bhāṣitam
c pratyuvāca śubhaṃ vākyaṃ sāntvayan parayā girā
a aśmavarṣeṇa mahatā bhṛtyās te vinipātitāḥ
c tvaṃ cāśramapade supto vātavarṣabhayārditaḥ
a samāśvasihi bhadraṃ te nirbhayo vigatajvaraḥ
c phalamūlāśano vīra vasa ceha yathāsukham
a sa rājā tena vākyena pratyāśvasto mahāyaśāḥ
c pratyuvāca śubhaṃ vākyaṃ dīno bhṛtyajanakṣayāt
a tyakṣyāmy ahaṃ svakaṃ rājyaṃ nāhaṃ bhṛtyair vinā kṛtaḥ
c vartayeyaṃ kṣaṇaṃ brahman samanujñātum arhasi
a suto dharmaparo brahmañ jyeṣṭho mama mahāyaśāḥ
c śaśabindur iti khyātaḥ sa me rājyaṃ prapatsyate
a na hi śakṣyāmy ahaṃ gatvā bhṛtyadārān sukhānvitān
c prativaktuṃ mahātejaḥ kiṃ cid apy aśubhaṃ vacaḥ
a tathā bruvati rājendre budhaḥ paramam adbhutam
c sāntvapūrvam athovāca vāsas ta iha rocatām
a na saṃtāpas tvayā kāryaḥ kārdameya mahābala
c saṃvatsaroṣitasyeha kārayiṣyāmi te hitam
a tasya tadvacanaṃ śrutvā budhasyākliṣṭakarmaṇaḥ
c vāsāya vidadhe buddhiṃ yad uktaṃ brahmavādinā
a māsaṃ sa strī tadā bhūtvā ramayaty aniśaṃ śubhā
c māsaṃ puruṣabhāvena dharmabuddhiṃ cakāra saḥ
a tataḥ sa navame māsi ilā somasutātmajam
c janayām āsa suśroṇī purūravasam ātmajam
a jātamātraṃ tu suśroṇī pitur haste nyaveśayat
c budhasya samavarṇābham ilāputraṃ mahābalam
a budho 'pi puruṣībhūtaṃ samāśvāsya narādhipam
c kathābhī ramayām āsa dharmayuktābhir ātmavān
a tathoktavati rāme tu tasya janma tad adbhutam
c uvāca lakṣmaṇo bhūyo bharataś ca mahāyaśāḥ
a sā priyā somaputrasya saṃvatsaram athoṣitā
c akarot kiṃ naraśreṣṭha tat tvaṃ śaṃsitum arhasi
a tayos tad vākyamādhuryaṃ niśamya paripṛcchatoḥ
c rāmaḥ punar uvācemāṃ prajāpatisute kathām
a puruṣatvaṃ gate śūre budhaḥ paramabuddhimān
c saṃvartaṃ paramodāram ājuhāva mahāyaśāḥ
a cyavanaṃ bhṛguputraṃ ca muniṃ cāriṣṭaneminam
c pramodanaṃ modakaraṃ tato durvāsasaṃ munim
a etān sarvān samānīya vākyajñas tattvadarśinaḥ
c uvāca sarvān suhṛdo dhairyeṇa susamāhitaḥ
a ayaṃ rājā mahābāhuḥ kardamasya ilaḥ sutaḥ
c jānītainaṃ yathā bhūtaṃ śreyo hy asya vidhīyatām
a teṣāṃ saṃvadatām eva tam āśramam upāgamat
c kardamaḥ sumahātejā dvijaiḥ saha mahātmabhiḥ
a pulastyaś ca kratuś caiva vaṣaṭkāras tathaiva ca
c oṃkāraś ca mahātejās tam āśramam upāgaman
a te sarve hṛṣṭamanasaḥ parasparasamāgame
c hitaiṣiṇo bāhli pateḥ pṛthag vākyam athābruvan
a kardamas tv abravīd vākyaṃ sutārthaṃ paramaṃ hitam
c dvijāḥ śṛṇuta madvākyaṃ yac chreyaḥ pārthivasya hi
a nānyaṃ paśyāmi bhaiṣajyam antareṇa vṛṣadhvajam
c nāśvamedhāt paro yajñaḥ priyaś caiva mahātmanaḥ
a tasmād yajāmahe sarve pārthivārthe durāsadam
c kardamenaivam uktās tu sarva eva dvijarṣabhāḥ
e rocayanti sma taṃ yajñaṃ rudrasyārādhanaṃ prati
a saṃvartasya tu rājarṣiḥ śiṣyaḥ parapuraṃjayaḥ
c marutta iti vikhyatas taṃ yajñaṃ samupāharat
a tato yajño mahān āsīd budhāśramasamīpataḥ
c rudraś ca paramaṃ toṣam ājagāma mahāyaśāḥ
a atha yajñasamāptau tu prītaḥ paramayā mudā
c umāpatir dvijān sarvān uvācedam ilāṃ prati
a prīto 'smi hayamedhena bhaktyā ca dvijasattamāḥ
c asya bāhlipateś caiva kiṃ karomi priyaṃ śubham
a tathā vadati deveśe dvijās te susamāhitāḥ
c prasādayanti deveśaṃ yathā syāt puruṣas tv ilā
a tataḥ prītamanā rudraḥ puruṣatvaṃ dadau punaḥ
c ilāyai sumahātejā dattvā cāntaradhīyata
a nivṛtte hayamedhe tu gate cādarśanaṃ hare
c yathāgataṃ dvijāḥ sarve agacchan dīrghadarśinaḥ
a rājā tu bāhlim utsṛjya madhyadeśe hy anuttamam
c niveśayām āsa puraṃ pratiṣṭhānaṃ yaśaskaram
a śaśabindus tu rājāsīd bāhlyāṃ parapuraṃjayaḥ
c pratiṣṭhāna ilo rājā prajāpatisuto balī
a sa kāle prāptavāṃl lokam ilo brāhmam anuttamam
c ailaḥ purūravā rājā pratiṣṭhānam avāptavān
a īdṛśo hy aśvamedhasya prabhāvaḥ puruṣarṣabhau
c strībhūtaḥ pauruṣaṃ lebhe yac cānyad api durlabham
a etad ākhyāya kākutstho bhrātṛhyām amitaprabhaḥ
c lakṣmaṇaṃ punār evāha dharmayuktam idaṃ vacaḥ
a vasiṣṭhaṃ vāmadevaṃ ca jābālim atha kaśyapam
c dvijāṃś ca sarvapravarān aśvamedhapuraskṛtān
a etān sarvān samāhūya mantrayitvā ca lakṣmaṇa
c hayaṃ lakṣmaṇasaṃpannaṃ vimokṣyāmi samādhinā
a tad vākyaṃ rāghaveṇoktaṃ śrutvā tvaritavikramaḥ
c dvijān sarvān samāhūya darśayām āsa rāghavam
a te dṛṣṭvā devasaṃkāśaṃ kṛtapādābhivandanam
c rāghavaṃ sudurādharṣam āśīrbhiḥ samapūjayan
a prāñjalis tu tato bhūtvā rāghavo dvijasāttamān
c uvāca dharmasaṃyuktam aśvamedhāśritaṃ vacaḥ
a sa teṣāṃ dvijamukhyānāṃ vākyam adbhutadarśanam
c aśvamedhāśritaṃ śrutvā bhṛśaṃ prīto 'bhavat tadā
a vijñāya tu mataṃ teṣāṃ rāmo lakṣmaṇam abravīt
c preṣayasva mahābāho sugrīvāya mahātmane
a śīghraṃ mahadbhir haribhir bahibhiś ca tadāśrayaiḥ
c sārdham āgaccha bhadraṃ te anubhoktuṃ makhottamam
a vibhīṣaṇaś ca rakṣobhiḥ kāmagair bahubhir vṛtaḥ
c aśvamedhaṃ mahābāhuḥ prāpnotu laghuvikramaḥ
a rājānaś ca naravyāghra ye me priyacikīrṣavaḥ
c sānugāḥ kṣipram āyāntu yajñabhūmim anuttamām
a deśāntaragatā ye ca dvijā dharmaparāyaṇāḥ
c nimantrayasva tān sarvān aśvamedhāya lakṣmaṇa
a ṛṣayaś cā mahābāho āhūyantāṃ tapodhanāḥ
c deśāntaragatā ye ca sadārāś ca maharṣayaḥ
a yajñavāṭaś ca sumahān gomatyā naimiṣe vane
c ājñāpyatāṃ mahābāho tad dhi puṇyam anuttamam
a śataṃ vāhasahasrāṇāṃ taṇḍulānāṃ vapuṣmatām
c ayutaṃ tilamudgasya prayātv agre mahābala
a suvarṇakoṭyo bahulā hiraṇyasya śatottarāḥ
c agrato bharataḥ kṛtvā gacchatv agre mahāmatiḥ
a antarāpaṇavīthyaś ca sarvāṃś ca naṭanartakān
c naigamān bālavṛddhāṃś ca dvijāṃś ca susamāhitān
a karmāntikāṃś ca kuśalāñ śilpinaś ca supaṇḍitān
c mātaraś caiva me sarvāḥ kumārāntaḥpurāṇi ca
a kāñcanīṃ mama patnīṃ ca dīkṣārhāṃ yajñakarmaṇi
c agrato bharataḥ kṛtvā gacchatv agre mahāmatiḥ
a tat sarvam akhilenāśu prasthāpya bharatāgrajaḥ
c hayaṃ lakṣmaṇasaṃpannaṃ kṛṣṇasāraṃ mumoca ha
a ṛtvigbhir lakṣmaṇaṃ sārdham aśve ca viniyujya saḥ
c tato 'bhyagacchat kākutsthaḥ saha sainyena naimiṣam
a yajñavāṭaṃ mahābāhur dṛṣṭvā paramam adbhutam
c praharṣam atulaṃ lebhe śrīmān iti ca so 'bravīt
a naimiṣe vasatas tasya sarva eva narādhipāḥ
c ājagmuḥ sarvarāṣṭrebhyas tān rāmaḥ pratyapūjayat
a upakāryān mahārhāṃś ca pārthivānāṃ mahātmanām
c sānugānāṃ naraśreṣṭho vyādideśa mahādyutiḥ
a annapānāni vastrāṇi sānugānāṃ mahātmanām
c bharataḥ saṃdadāv āśu śatrughnasahitas tadā
a vānarāś ca mahātmānaḥ sugrīvasahitās tadā
c viprāṇāṃ praṇatāḥ sarve cakrire pariveṣaṇam
a vibhīṣaṇaś ca rakṣobhiḥ sragvibhir bahubhir vṛtaḥ
c ṛṣīṇām ugratapasāṃ kiṃkaraḥ paryupasthitaḥ
a evaṃ suvihito yajño hayamedho 'bhyavartata
c lakṣmaṇenābhiguptā ca hayacaryā pravartitā
a nānyaḥ śabdo 'bhavat tatra hayamedhe mahātmanaḥ
c chandato dehi visrabdho yāvat tuṣyanti yācakāḥ
e tāvad vānararakṣobhir dattam evābhyadṛśyata
a na kaś cin malinas tatra dīno vāpy atha vā kṛśaḥ
c tasmin yajñavare rājño hṛṣṭapuṣṭajanāvṛte
a ye ca tatra mahātmāno munayaś cirajīvinaḥ
c nāsmaraṃs tādṛśaṃ yajñaṃ dānaughasamalaṃkṛtam
a rajatānāṃ suvarṇānāṃ ratnānām atha vāsasām
c aniśaṃ dīyamānānāṃ nāntaḥ samupadṛśyate
a na śakrasya na somasya yamasya varuṇasya vā
c īdṛśo dṛṣṭapūrvo na evam ūcus tapodhanāḥ
a sarvatra vānarās tasthuḥ sarvatraiva ca rākṣasāḥ
c vāso dhanāni kāmibhyaḥ pūrṇahastā dadur bhṛśam
a īdṛśo rājasiṃhasya yajñaḥ sarvaguṇānvitaḥ
c saṃvatsaram atho sāgraṃ vartate na ca hīyate
a vartamāne tathābhūte yajñe paramake 'dbhute
c saśiṣya ājagāmāśu vālmīkir munipuṃgavaḥ
a sa dṛṣṭvā divyasaṃkāśaṃ yajñam adbhutadarśanam
c ekānte ṛṣivāṭānāṃ cakāra uṭajāñ śubhān
a sa śiṣyāv abravīd dhṛṣṭo yuvāṃ gatvā samāhitau
c kṛtsnaṃ rāmāyaṇaṃ kāvyaṃ gāyatāṃ parayā mudā
a ṛṣivāṭeṣu puṇyeṣu brāhmaṇāvasatheṣu ca
c rathyāsu rājamārgeṣu pārthivānāṃ gṛheṣu ca
a rāmasya bhavanadvāri yatra karma ca vartate
c ṛtvijām agrataś caiva tatra geyaṃ viśeṣataḥ
a imāni ca phalāny atra svādūni vividhāni ca
c jātāni parvatāgreṣu āsvādyāsvādya gīyatām
a na yāsyathaḥ śramaṃ vatsau bhakṣayitvā phalāni vai
c mūlāni ca sumṛṣṭāni nagarāt parihāsyatha
a yadi śabdāpayed rāmaḥ śravaṇāya mahīpatiḥ
c ṛṣīṇām upaviṣṭānāṃ tato geyaṃ pravartatām
a divase viṃśatiḥ sargā geyā vai parayā mudā
c pramāṇair bahubhis tatra yathoddiṣṭaṃ mayā purā
a lobhaś cāpi na kartavyaḥ svalpo 'pi dhanakāṅkṣayā
c kiṃ dhanenāśramasthānāṃ phalamūlopabhoginām
a yadi pṛcchet sa kākutstho yuvāṃ kasyeti dārakau
c vālmīker atha śiṣyau hi brūtām evaṃ narādhipam
a imās tantrīḥ sumadhurāḥ sthānaṃ vā pūrvadarśitam
c mūrchayitvā sumadhuraṃ gāyetāṃ vigatajvarau
a ādiprabhṛti geyaṃ syān na cāvajñāya pārthivam
c pitā hi sarvabhūtānāṃ rājā bhavati dharmataḥ
a tad yuvāṃ hṛṣṭamanasau śvaḥ prabhāte samādhinā
c gāyetāṃ madhuraṃ geyaṃ tantrīlayasamanvitam
a iti saṃdiśya bahuśo muniḥ prācetasas tadā
c vālmīkiḥ paramodāras tūṣṇīm āsīn mahāyaśāḥ
a tām adbhutāṃ tau hṛdaye kumārau
niveśya vāṇīm ṛṣibhāṣitāṃ śubhām
c samutsukau tau sukham ūṣatur niśāṃ
yathāśvinau bhārgavanītisaṃskṛtau
a tau rajanyāṃ prabhātāyāṃ snātau hutahutāśanau
c yathoktam ṛṣiṇā pūrvaṃ tatra tatrābhyagāyatām
a tāṃ sa śuśrāva kākutsthaḥ pūrvacaryāṃ tatas tataḥ
c apūrvāṃ pāṭhya jātiṃ ca geyena samalaṃkṛtām
a pramāṇair bahubhir baddhāṃ tantrīlayasamanvitām
c bālābhyāṃ rāghavaḥ śrutvā kautūhalaparo 'bhavat
a atha karmāntare rājā samānīya mahāmunīn
c pārthivāṃś ca naravyāghraḥ paṇḍitān naigamāṃs tathā
a paurāṇikāñ śabdavito ye ca vṛddhā dvijātayaḥ
c etān sarvān samānīya gātārau samaveśayat
a hṛṣṭā ṛṣigaṇās tatra pārthivāś ca mahaujasaḥ
c pibanta iva cakṣurbhyāṃ rājānaṃ gāyakau ca tau
a parasparam athocus te sarva eva samaṃ tataḥ
c ubhau rāmasya sadṛśau bimbād bimbam ivoddhṛtau
a jaṭilau yadi na syātāṃ na valkaladharau yadi
c viśeṣaṃ nādhigacchāmo gāyato rāghavasya ca
a teṣāṃ saṃvadatām evaṃ śrotṝṇāṃ harṣavardhanam
c geyaṃ pracakratus tatra tāv ubhau munidārakau
a tataḥ pravṛttaṃ madhuraṃ gāndharvam atimānuṣam
c na ca tṛptiṃ yayuḥ sarve śrotāro geya saṃpadā
a pravṛttam āditaḥ pūrvaṃ sargān nāradadarśanāt
c tataḥ prabhṛti sargāṃś ca yāvadviṃśaty agāyatām
a tato 'parāhṇasamaye rāghavaḥ samabhāṣata
c śrutvā viṃśatisargāṃs tān bharataṃ bhrātṛvatsalaḥ
a aṣṭādaśa sahasrāṇi suvarṇasya mahātmanoḥ
c dadasva śīghraṃ kākutstha bālayor mā vṛthā śramaḥ
a dīyamānaṃ suvarṇaṃ tan nāgṛhṇītāṃ kuśīlavau
c ūcatuś ca mahātmānau kim aneneti vismitau
a vanyena phalamūlena niratu svo vanaukasau
c suvarṇena hiraṇyena kiṃ kariṣyāvahe vane
a tathā tayoḥ prabruvatoḥ kautūhalasamanvitāḥ
c śrotāraś caiva rāmaś ca sarva eva suvismitāḥ
a tasya caivāgamaṃ rāmaḥ kāvyasya śrotum utsukaḥ
c papraccha tau mahātejās tāv ubhau munidārakau
a kiṃpramāṇam idaṃ kāvyaṃ kā pratiṣṭhā mahātmanaḥ
c kartā kāvyasya mahataḥ ko vāsau munipuṃgavaḥ
a pṛcchantaṃ rāghavaṃ vākyam ūcatur munidārakau
c vālmīkir bhagavān kartā saṃprāpto yajñasaṃnidhim
e yenedaṃ caritaṃ tubhyam aśeṣaṃ saṃpradarśitam
a ādiprabhṛti rājendra pañcasarga śatāni ca
c pratiṣṭhā jīvitaṃ yāvat tāvad rājañ śubhāśubham
a yadi buddhiḥ kṛtā rājañ śravaṇāya mahāratha
c karmāntare kṣaṇī hūtas tac chṛṇuṣva sahānujaḥ
a bāḍham ity abravīd rāmas tau cānujñāpya rāghavam
c prahṛṣṭau jagmatur vāsaṃ yatrāsau munipuṃgavaḥ
a rāmo 'pi munibhiḥ sārdhaṃ pārthivaiś ca mahātmabhiḥ
c śrutvā tad gītamādhuryaṃ karmaśālām upāgamat
a rāmo bahūny ahāny eva tad gītaṃ paramādbhutam
c śuśrāva munibhiḥ sārdhaṃ rājabhiḥ saha vānaraiḥ
a tasmin gīte tu vijñāya sītāputrau kuśīlavau
c tasyāḥ pariṣado madhye rāmo vacanam abravīt
a madvaco brūta gacchadhvam iti bhagavato 'ntikam
a yadi śuddhasamācārā yadi vā vītakalmaṣā
c karotv ihātmanaḥ śuddhim anumānya mahāmunim
a chandaṃ munes tu vijñāya sītāyāś ca manogatam
c pratyayaṃ dātukāmāyās tataḥ śaṃsata me laghu
a śvaḥ prabhāte tu śapathaṃ maithilī janakātmajā
c karotu pariṣanmadhye śodhanārthaṃ mameha ca
a śrutvā tu rāghavasyaitad vacaḥ paramam adbhutam
c dūtāḥ saṃprayayur vāṭaṃ yatrāste munipuṃgavaḥ
a te praṇamya mahātmānaṃ jvalantam amitaprabham
c ūcus te rāma vākyāni mṛdūni madhurāṇi ca
a teṣāṃ tad bhāṣitaṃ śrutvā rāmasya ca manogatam
c vijñāya sumahātejā munir vākyam athābravīt
a evaṃ bhavatu bhadraṃ vo yathā tuṣyati rāghavaḥ
c tathā kariṣyate sītā daivataṃ hi patiḥ striyāḥ
a tathoktā muninā sarve rāmadūtā mahaujasaḥ
c pratyetya rāghavaṃ sarve munivākyaṃ babhāṣire
a tataḥ prahṛṣṭaḥ kākutsthaḥ śrutvā vākyaṃ mahātmanaḥ
c ṛṣīṃs tatra sametāṃś ca rājñaś caivābhyabhāṣata
a bhagavantaḥ saśiṣyā vai sānugaś ca narādhipāḥ
c paśyantu sītāśapathaṃ yaś caivānyo 'bhikāṅkṣate
a tasya tadvacanaṃ śrutvā rāghavasya mahātmanaḥ
c sarveṣam ṛṣimukhyānāṃ sādhuvādo mahān abhūt
a rājānaś ca mahātmānaḥ praśaṃsanti sma rāghavam
c upapannaṃ naraśreṣṭha tvayy eva bhuvi nānyataḥ
a evaṃ viniścayaṃ kṛtvā śvobhūta iti rāghavaḥ
c visarjayām āsa tadā sarvāṃs tāñ śatrusūdanaḥ
a tasyāṃ rajanyāṃ vyuṣṭāyāṃ yajñavāṭagato nṛpaḥ
c ṛṣīn sarvān mahātejāḥ śabdāpayati rāghavaḥ
a vasiṣṭho vāmadevaś ca jābālir atha kāśyapaḥ
c viśvāmitro dīrghatapā durvāsāś ca mahātapāḥ
a agastyo 'tha tathāśaktir bhārgavaś caiva vāmanaḥ
c mārkaṇḍeyaś ca dīrghāyur maudgalyaś ca mahātapāḥ
a bhārgavaś cyavanaś caiva śatānandaś ca dharmavit
c bharadvājaś ca tejasvī agniputraś ca suprabhaḥ
a ete cānye ca munayo bahavaḥ saṃśitavratāḥ
c rājānaś ca naravyāghrāḥ sarva eva samāgatāḥ
a rākṣasāś ca mahāvīryā vānarāś ca mahābalāḥ
c samājagmur mahātmānaḥ sarva eva kutūhalāt
a kṣatriyāś caiva vaiśyāś ca śūdrāś caiva sahasraśaḥ
c sītāśapathavīkṣārthaṃ sarva eva samāgatāḥ
a tathā samāgataṃ sarvam aśvabhūtam ivācalam
c śrutvā munivaras tūrṇaṃ sasītaḥ samupāgamat
a tam ṛṣiṃ pṛṣṭhataḥ sītā sānvagacchad avāṅmukhī
c kṛtāñjalir bāṣpagalā kṛtvā rāmaṃ manogatam
a tāṃ dṛṣṭvā śrīm ivāyāntīṃ brahmāṇam anugāminīm
c vālmīkeḥ pṛṣṭhataḥ sītāṃ sādhukāro mahān abhūt
a tato halahalā śabdaḥ sarveṣām evam ābabhau
c duḥkhajena viśālena śokenākulitātmanām
a sādhu sīteti ke cit tu sādhu rāmeti cāpare
c ubhāv eva tu tatrānye sādhu sādhv iti cābruvan
a tato madhyaṃ janaughānāṃ praviśya munipuṃgavaḥ
c sītāsahāyo vālmīkir iti hovāca rāghavam
a iyaṃ dāśarathe sītā suvratā dharmacāriṇī
c apāpā te parityaktā mamāśramasamīpataḥ
a lokāpavādabhītasya tava rāma mahāvrata
c pratyayaṃ dāsyate sītā tām anujñātum arhasi
a imau ca jānakī putrāv ubhau ca yamajātakau
c sutau tavaiva durdharṣo satyam etad bravīmi te
a pracetaso 'haṃ daśamaḥ putro rāghavanandana
c na smarāmy anṛtaṃ vākyaṃ tathemau tava putrakau
a bahuvarṣasahasrāṇi tapaścaryā mayā kṛtā
c tasyāḥ phalam upāśnīyām apāpā maithilī yathā
a ahaṃ pañcasu bhūteṣu manaḥṣaṣṭheṣu rāghava
c vicintya sītāṃ śuddheti nyagṛhṇāṃ vananirjhare
a iyaṃ śuddhasamācārā apāpā patidevatā
c lokāpavādabhītasya dāsyati pratyayaṃ tava
a vālmīkinaivam uktas tu rāghavaḥ pratyabhāṣata
c prāñjalir jagato madhye dṛṣṭvā tāṃ devavarṇinīm
a evam etan mahābhāga yathā vadasi dharmavit
c pratyayo hi mama brahmaṃs tava vākyair akalmaṣaiḥ
a pratyayo hi purā datto vaidehyā surasaṃnidhau
c seyaṃ lokabhayād brahmann apāpety abhijānatā
e parityaktā mayā sītā tad bhavān kṣantum arhati
a jānāmi cemau putrau me yamajātau kuśīlavau
c śuddhāyāṃ jagato madhye maithilyāṃ prītir astu me
a abhiprāyaṃ tu vijñāya rāmasya surasattamāḥ
c pitāmahaṃ puraskṛtya sarva eva samāgatāḥ
a ādityā vasavo rudrā viśve deśā marudgaṇāḥ
c aśvināv ṛṣigandharvā apsarāṇāṃ gaṇās tathā
e sādhyāś ca devāḥ sarve te sarve ca paramarṣayaḥ
a tato vāyuḥ śubhaḥ puṇyo divyagandho manoramaḥ
c taṃ janaughaṃ suraśreṣṭho hlādayām āsa sarvataḥ
a tad adbhutam ivācintyaṃ nirīkṣante samāhitāḥ
c mānavāḥ sarvarāṣṭrebhyaḥ pūrvaṃ kṛtayuge yathā
a sarvān samāgatān dṛṣṭvā sītā kāṣāyavāsinī
c abravīt prāñjalir vākyam adhodṛṣṭir avānmukhī
a yathāhaṃ rāghavād anyaṃ manasāpi na cintaye
c tathā me mādhavī devī vivaraṃ dātum arhati
a tathā śapantyāṃ vaidehyāṃ prādurāsīt tad adbhutam
c bhūtalād utthitaṃ divyaṃ siṃhāsanam anuttamam
a dhriyamāṇaṃ śirobhis tan nāgair amitavikramaiḥ
c divyaṃ divyena vapuṣā sarvaratnavibhūṣitam
a tasmiṃs tu dharaṇī devī bāhubhyāṃ gṛhya maithilīm
c svāgatenābhinandyainām āsane copaveṣayat
a tām āsanagatāṃ dṛṣṭvā praviśantīṃ rasātalam
c puṇyavṛṣṭir avicchinnā divyā sītām avākirat
a sādhukāraś ca sumahān devānāṃ sahasotthitaḥ
c sādhu sādhv iti vai sīte yasyās te śīlam īdṛśam
a evaṃ bahuvidhā vāco hy antarikṣagatāḥ surāḥ
c vyājahrur hṛṣṭamanaso dṛṣṭvā sītāpraveśanam
a yajñavāṭagatāś cāpi munayaḥ sarva eva te
c rājānaś ca naravyāghrā vismayān noparemire
a antarikṣe ca bhūmau ca sarve sthāvarajaṅgamāḥ
c dānavāś ca mahākāyāḥ pātāle pannagādhipāḥ
a ke cid vineduḥ saṃhṛṣṭāḥ ke cid dhyānaparāyaṇāḥ
c ke cid rāmaṃ nirīkṣante ke cit sītām acetanāḥ
a sītāpraveśanaṃ dṛṣṭvā teṣām āsīt samāgamaḥ
c taṃ muhūrtam ivātyarthaṃ sarvaṃ saṃmohitaṃ jagat
a tadāvasāne yajñasya rāmaḥ paramadurmanāḥ
c apaśyamāno vaidehīṃ mene śūnyam idaṃ jagat
e śokena paramāyatto na śāntiṃ manasāgamat
a visṛjya pārthivān sarvān ṛkṣavānararākṣasān
c janaughaṃ brahmamukhyānāṃ vittapūrṇaṃ vyasarjayat
a tato visṛjya tān sarvān rāmo rājīvalocanaḥ
c hṛdi kṛtvā tadā sītām ayodhyāṃ praviveśa saḥ
a na sītāyāḥ parāṃ bhāryāṃ vavre sa raghunandanaḥ
c yajñe yajñe ca patnyarthaṃ jānakī kāñcanī bhavat
a daśavarṣasahasrāṇi vājimedham upākarot
c vājapeyān daśaguṇāṃs tathā bahusuvarṇakān
a agniṣṭomātirātrābhyāṃ gosavaiś ca mahādhanaiḥ
c īje kratubhir anyaiś ca sa śrīmān āptadakṣiṇaiḥ
a evaṃ sa kālaḥ sumahān rājyasthasya mahātmanaḥ
c dharme prayatamānasya vyatīyād rāghavasya tu
a ṛkṣavānararakṣāṃsi sthitā rāmasya śāsane
c anurajyanti rājāno ahany ahani rāghavam
a kāle varṣati parjanyaḥ subhikṣaṃ vimalā diśaḥ
c hṛṣṭapuṣṭajanākīrṇaṃ puraṃ janapadas tathā
a nākāle mriyate kaś cin na vyādhiḥ prāṇināṃ tadā
c nādharmaś cābhavat kaś cid rāme rājyaṃ praśāsati
a atha dīrghasya kālasya rāmamātā yaśasvinī
c putrapautraiḥ parivṛtā kāladharmam upāgamat
a anviyāya sumitrāpi kaikeyī ca yaśasvinī
c dharmaṃ kṛtvā bahuvidhaṃ tridive paryavasthitā
a sarvāḥ pratiṣṭhitāḥ svarge rājñā daśarathena ca
c samāgatā mahābhāgāḥ saha dharmaṃ ca lebhire
a tāsāṃ rāmo mahādānaṃ kāle kāle prayacchati
c mātṝṇām aviśeṣeṇa brāhmaṇeṣu tapasviṣu
a pitryāṇi bahuratnāni yajñān paramadustarān
c cakāra rāmo dharmātmā pitṝn devān vivardhayan
a kasya cit tv atha kālasya yudhājit kekayo nṛpaḥ
c svaguruṃ preṣayām āsa rāghavāya mahātmane
a gārgyam aṅgirasaḥ putraṃ brahmarṣim amitaprabham
c daśa cāśvasahasrāṇi prītidānam anuttamam
a kambalāni ca ratnāni citravastram athottamam
c rāmāya pradadau rājā bahūny ābharaṇāni ca
a śrutvā tu rāghavo gārgyaṃ maharṣiṃ samupāgatam
c mātulasyāśvapatinaḥ priyaṃ dūtam upāgatam
a pratyudgamya ca kākutsthaḥ krośamātraṃ sahānugaḥ
c gārgyaṃ saṃpūjayām āsa dhanaṃ tat pratigṛhya ca
a pṛṣṭvā ca prītidaṃ sarvaṃ kuśalaṃ mātulasya ca
c upaviṣṭaṃ mahābhāgaṃ rāmaḥ praṣṭuṃ pracakrame
a kim āha matulo vākyaṃ yadarthaṃ bhagavān iha
c prāpto vākyavidāṃ śreṣṭha sākṣād iva bṛhaspatiḥ
a rāmasya bhāṣitaṃ śrutvā brahmarṣiḥ kāryavistaram
c vaktum adbhutasaṃkāśaṃ rāghavāyopacakrame
a mātulas te mahābāho vākyam āha nararṣabha
c yudhājit prītisaṃyuktaṃ śrūyatāṃ yadi rocate
a ayaṃ gandharvaviṣayaḥ phalamūlopaśobhitaḥ
c sindhor ubhayataḥ pārśve deśaḥ paramaśobhanaḥ
a taṃ ca rakṣanti gandharvāḥ sāyudhā yuddhakovidāḥ
c śailūṣasya sutā vīrās tisraḥ koṭyo mahābalāḥ
a tān vinirjitya kākutstha gandharvaviṣayaṃ śubham
c niveśaya mahābāho dve pure susamāhitaḥ
a anyasya na gatis tatra deśaś cāyaṃ suśobhanaḥ
c rocatāṃ te mahābāho nāhaṃ tvām anṛtaṃ vade
a tac chrutvā rāghavaḥ prīto mararṣir mātulasya ca
c uvāca bāḍham ity evaṃ bharataṃ cānvavaikṣata
a so 'bravīd rāghavaḥ prītaḥ prāñjalipragraho dvijam
c imau kumārau taṃ deśaṃ brahmarṣe vijayiṣyataḥ
a bharatasyātmajau vīrau takṣaḥ puṣkala eva ca
c mātulena suguptau tau dharmeṇa ca samāhitau
a bharataṃ cāgrataḥ kṛtvā kumārau sabalānugau
c nihatya gandharvasutān dve pure vibhajiṣyataḥ
a niveśya te puravare ātmājau saṃniveśya ca
c āgamiṣyati me bhūyaḥ sakāśam atidhārmikaḥ
a brahmarṣim evam uktvā tu bharataṃ sabalānugam
c ājñāpayām āsa tadā kumārau cābhyaṣecayat
a nakṣatreṇa ca saumyena puraskṛtyāṅgiraḥ sutam
c bharataḥ saha sainyena kumārābhyāṃ ca niryayau
a sā senā śakrayukteva naragān niryayāv atha
c rāghavānugatā dūraṃ durādharṣā surāsuraiḥ
