a māṃsāśīni ca sattvāni rakṣāṃsi sumahānti ca
c anujagmuś ca bharataṃ rudhirasya pipāsayā
a bhūtagrāmāś ca bahavo māṃsabhakṣāḥ sudāruṇāḥ
c gandharvaputramāṃsāni bhoktukāmāḥ sahasraśaḥ
a siṃhavyāghrasṛgālānāṃ khecarāṇāṃ ca pakṣiṇām
c bahūni vai sahasrāṇi senāyā yayur agrataḥ
a adhyardhamāsam uṣitā pathi senā nirāmayā
c hṛṣṭapuṣṭajanākīrṇā kekayaṃ samupāgamat
a śrutvā senāpatiṃ prāptaṃ bharataṃ kekayādhipaḥ
c yudhājid gārgyasahitaṃ parāṃ prītim upāgamat
a sa niryayau janaughena mahatā kekayādhipaḥ
c tvaramāṇo 'bhicakrāma gandharvān devarūpiṇaḥ
a bharataś ca yudhājic ca sametau laghuvikramau
c gandharvanagaraṃ prāptau sabalau sapadānugau
a śrutvā tu bharataṃ prāptaṃ gandharvās te samāgatāḥ
c yoddhukāmā mahāvīryā vinadantaḥ samantataḥ
a tataḥ samabhavad yuddhaṃ tumulaṃ lomaharṣaṇam
c saptarātraṃ mahābhīmaṃ na cānyatarayor jayaḥ
a tato rāmānujaḥ kruddhaḥ kālasyāstraṃ sudāruṇam
c saṃvartaṃ nāma bharato gandharveṣv abhyayojayat
a te baddhāḥ kālapāśena saṃvartena vidāritāḥ
c kṣaṇenābhihatās tisras tatra koṭyo mahātmanā
a taṃ ghātaṃ ghorasaṃkāśaṃ na smaranti divaukasaḥ
c nimeṣāntaramātreṇa tādṛśānāṃ mahātmanām
a hateṣu teṣu vīreṣu bharataḥ kaikayīsutaḥ
c niveśayām āsa tadā samṛddhe dve purottame
e takṣaṃ takṣaśilāyāṃ tu puṣkaraṃ puṣkarāvatau
a gandharvadeśo ruciro gāndhāraviṣayaś ca saḥ
c varṣaiḥ pañcabhir ākīrṇo viṣayair nāgarais tathā
a dhanaratnaughasaṃpūrṇo kānanair upaśobhite
c anyonyasaṃgharṣakṛte spardhayā guṇavistare
a ubhe suruciraprakhye vyavahārair akalmaṣaiḥ
c udyānayānaughavṛte suvibhaktāntarāpaṇe
a ubhe puravare ramye vistarair upaśobhite
c gṛhamukhyaiḥ surucirair vimānaiḥ samavarṇibhiḥ
a śobhite śobhanīyaiś ca devāyatanavistaraiḥ
c niveśya pañcabhir varṣair bharato rāghavānujaḥ
e punar āyān mahābāhur ayodhyāṃ kaikayīsutaḥ
a so 'bhivādya mahātmānaṃ sākṣād dharmam ivāparam
c rāghavaṃ bharataḥ śrīmān brahmāṇam iva vāsavaḥ
a śaśaṃsa ca yathāvṛttaṃ gandharvavadham uttamam
c niveśanaṃ ca deśasya śrutvā prīto 'sya rāghavaḥ
a tac chrutvā harṣam āpede rāghavo bhrātṛbhiḥ saha
c vākyaṃ cādbhutasaṃkāśaṃ bhrātṝn provāca rāghavaḥ
a imau kumārau saumitre tava dharmaviśāradau
c aṅgadaś candraketuś ca rājyārhau dṛḍhadhanvinau
a imau rājye 'bhiṣekṣyāmi deśaḥ sādhu vidhīyatām
c ramaṇīyo hy asaṃbādho rametāṃ yatra dhanvinau
a na rājñāṃ yatra pīdā syān nāśramāṇāṃ vināśanam
c sa deśo dṛśyatāṃ saumya nāparādhyāmahe yathā
a tathoktavati rāme tu bharataḥ pratyuvāca ha
c ayaṃ kārāpatho deśaḥ suramaṇyo nirāmayaḥ
a niveśyatāṃ tatra puram aṅgadasya mahātmanaḥ
c candraketoś ca ruciraṃ candrakāntaṃ nirāmayam
a tad vākyaṃ bharatenoktaṃ pratijagrāha rāghavaḥ
c taṃ ca kṛtā vaśe deśam aṅgadasya nyaveśayat
a aṅgadīyā purī ramyā aṅgadasya niveśitā
c ramaṇīyā suguptā ca rāmeṇākliṣṭakarmaṇā
a candraketus tu mallasya mallabhūmyāṃ niveśitā
c candrakānteti vikhyātā divyā svargapurī yathā
a tato rāmaḥ parāṃ prītiṃ bharato lakṣmaṇas tathā
c yayur yudhi durādharṣā abhiṣekaṃ ca cakrire
a abhiṣicya kumārau dvau prasthāpya sabalānugau
c aṅgadaṃ paścimā bhūmiṃ candraketum udaṅmukham
a aṅgadaṃ cāpi saumitrir lakṣmaṇo 'nujagāma ha
c candraketos tu bharataḥ pārṣṇigrāho babhūva ha
a lakṣmaṇas tv aṅgadīyāyāṃ saṃvatsaram athoṣitaḥ
c putre sthite durādharṣe ayodhyāṃ punar āgamat
a bharato 'pi tathaivoṣya saṃvatsaram athādhikam
c ayodhyāṃ punar agamya rāmapādāv upāgamat
a ubhau saumitribharatau rāmapādāv anuvratau
c kālaṃ gatam api snehān na jajñāte 'tidhārmikau
a evaṃ varṣasahasrāṇi daśateṣāṃ yayus tadā
c dharme prayatamānānāṃ paurakāryeṣu nityadā
a vihṛtya lākaṃ paripūrṇamānasāḥ
śriyā vṛtā dharmapathe pare sthitāḥ
c trayaḥ samiddhā iva dīptatejasā
hutāgnayaḥ sādhu mahādhvare trayaḥ
a kasya cit tv atha kālasya rāme dharmapathe sthite
c kālas tāpasarūpeṇa rājadvāram upāgamat
a so 'bravīl lakṣmaṇaṃ vākyaṃ dhṛtimantaṃ yaśasvinam
c māṃ nivedaya rāmāya saṃprāptaṃ kāryagauravāt
a dūto hy atibalasyāhaṃ maharṣer amitaujasaḥ
c rāmaṃ didṛkṣur āyātaḥ kāryeṇa hi mahābala
a tasya tadvacanaṃ śrutvā saumitris tvarayānvitaḥ
c nyavedayata rāmāya tāpasasya vivakṣitam
a jayasva rājan dharmeṇa ubhau lokau mahādyute
c dūtas tvāṃ draṣṭum āyātas tapasvī bhāskaraprabhaḥ
a tad vākyaṃ lakṣmaṇenoktaṃ śrutvā rāma uvāca ha
c praveśyatāṃ munis tāta mahaujās tasya vākyadhṛk
a saumitris tu tathety uktvā prāveśayata taṃ munim
c jvalantam iva tejobhiḥ pradahantam ivāṃśubhiḥ
a so 'bhigamya raghuśreṣṭhaṃ dīpyamānaṃ svatejasā
c ṛṣir madhurayā vācā vardhasvety āha rāghavam
a tasmai rāmo mahātejāḥ pūjām arghya purogamām
c dadau kuśalam avyagraṃ praṣṭuṃ caivopacakrame
a pṛṣṭhaś ca kuśalaṃ tena rāmeṇa vadatāṃ varaḥ
c āsane kāñcane divye niṣasāda mahāyaśāḥ
a tam uvāca tato rāmaḥ svāgataṃ te mahāmune
c prāpayasva ca vākyāni yato dūtas tvam āgataḥ
a codito rājasiṃhena munir vākyam udīrayat
c dvandvam etat pravaktavyaṃ na ca cakṣur hataṃ vacaḥ
a yaḥ śṛṇoti nirīkṣed vā sa vadhyas tava rāghava
c bhaved vai munimukhyasya vacanaṃ yady avekṣase
a tatheti ca pratijñāya rāmo lakṣmaṇam abravīt
c dvāri tiṣṭha mahābāho pratihāraṃ visarjaya
a sa me vadhyaḥ khalu bhavet kathāṃ dvandvasamīritām
c ṛṣer mama ca saumitre paśyed vā śṛṇuyā ca yaḥ
a tato nikṣipya kākutstho lakṣmaṇaṃ dvārasaṃgrahe
c tam uvāca muniṃ vākyaṃ kathayasveti rāghavaḥ
a yat te manīṣitaṃ vākyaṃ yena vāsi samāhitaḥ
c kathayasva viśaṅkas tvaṃ mamāpi hṛdi vartate
a śṛṇu rāma mahābāho yadartham aham āhataḥ
c pitāmahena devena preṣito 'smi mahābala
a tavāhaṃ pūrvake bhāve putraḥ parapuraṃjaya
c māyāsaṃbhāvito vīra kālaḥ sarvasamāharaḥ
a pitāmahaś ca bhagavān āha lokapatiḥ prabhuḥ
c samayas te mahābāho svarlokān parirakṣitum
a saṃkṣipya ca purā lokān māyayā svayam eva hi
c mahārṇave śayāno 'psu māṃ tvaṃ pūrvam ajījanaḥ
a bhogavantaṃ tato nāgam anantam udake śayam
c māyayā janayitvā tvaṃ dvau ca sattvau mahābalau
a madhuṃ ca kaiṭabhaṃ caiva yayor asthicayair vṛtā
c iyaṃ parvatasaṃbādhā medinī cābhavan mahī
a padme divyārkasaṃkāśe nābhyām utpādya mām api
c prājāpatyaṃ tvayā karma sarvaṃ mayi niveśitam
a so 'haṃ saṃnyastabhāro hi tvām upāse jagatpatim
c rakṣāṃ vidhatsva bhūteṣu mama tejaḥ karo bhavān
a tatas tvam api durdharṣas tasmād bhāvāt sanātanāt
c rakṣārthaṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ viṣṇutvam upajagmivān
a adityāṃ vīryavān putro bhrātṝṇāṃ harṣavardhanaḥ
c samutpanneṣu kṛtyeṣu lokasāhyāya kalpase
a sa tvaṃ vitrāsyamānāsu prajāsu jagatāṃ vara
c rāvaṇasya vadhākāṅkṣī mānuṣeṣu mano 'dadhāḥ
a daśavarṣasahasrāṇi daśavarṣaśatāni ca
c kṛtvā vāsasya niyatiṃ svayam evātmanaḥ purā
a sa tvaṃ manomayaḥ putraḥ pūrṇāyur mānuṣeṣv iha
c kālo naravaraśreṣṭha samīpam upavartitum
a yadi bhūyo mahārāja prajā icchasy upāsitum
c vasa vā vīra bhadraṃ te evam āha pitāmahaḥ
a atha vā vijigīṣā te suralokāya rāghava
c sanāthā viṣṇunā devā bhavantu vigatajvarāḥ
a śrutvā pitāmahenoktaṃ vākyaṃ kālasamīritam
c rāghavaḥ prahasan vākyaṃ sarvasaṃhāram abravīt
a śrutaṃ me devadevasya vākyaṃ paramam adbhutam
c prītir hi mahatī jātā tavāgamanasaṃbhavā
a bhadraṃ te 'stu gamiṣyāmi yata evāham āgataḥ
c hṛd gato hy asi saṃprāpto na me 'sty atra vicāraṇā
a mayā hi sarvakṛtyeṣu devānāṃ vaśavartinām
c sthātavyaṃ sarvasaṃhāre yathā hy āha pitāmahaḥ
a tathā tayoḥ kathayator durvāsā bhagavān ṛṣiḥ
c rāmasya darśanākāṅkṣī rājadvāram upāgamat
a so 'bhigamya ca saumitrim uvāca ṛṣisattamaḥ
c rāmaṃ darśaya me śīghraṃ purā me 'rtho 'tivartate
a munes tu bhāṣitaṃ śrutvā lakṣmaṇaḥ paravīrahā
c abhivādya mahātmānaṃ vākyam etad uvāca ha
a kiṃ kāryaṃ brūhi bhagavan ko vārthaḥ kiṃ karomy aham
c vyagro hi rāghavo brahman muhūrtaṃ vā pratīkṣatām
a tac chrutvā ṛṣiśārdūlaḥ krodhena kaluṣīkṛtaḥ
c uvāca lakṣmaṇaṃ vākyaṃ nirdahann iva cakṣuṣā
a asmin kṣaṇe māṃ saumitre rāmāya prativedaya
c viṣayaṃ tvāṃ puraṃ caiva śapiṣye rāghavaṃ tathā
a bharataṃ caiva saumitre yuṣmākaṃ yā ca saṃtatiḥ
c na hi śakṣyāmy ahaṃ bhūyo manyuṃ dhārayituṃ hṛdi
a tac chrutvā ghorasaṃkāśaṃ vākyaṃ tasya mahātmanaḥ
c cintayām āsa manasā tasya vākyasya niścayam
a ekasya maraṇaṃ me 'stu mā bhūt sarvavināśanam
c iti buddhyā viniścitya rāghavāya nyavedayat
a lakṣmaṇasya vacaḥ śrutvā rāmaḥ kālaṃ visṛjya ca
c niṣpatya tvaritaṃ rājā atreḥ putraṃ dadarśa ha
a so 'bhivādya mahātmānaṃ jvalantam iva tejasā
c kiṃ kāryam iti kākutsthaḥ kṛtāñjalir abhāṣata
a tad vākyaṃ rāghaveṇṇoktaṃ śrutvā munivaraḥ prabhuḥ
c pratyāha rāmaṃ durvāsāḥ śrūyatāṃ dharmavatsala
a adya varṣasahasrasya samāptir mama rāghava
c so 'haṃ bhojanam icchāmi yathāsiddhaṃ tavānagha
a tac chrutvā vacanaṃ rāmo harṣeṇa mahatānvitaḥ
c bhojanaṃ munimukhyāya yathāsiddham upāharat
a sa tu bhuktvā muniśreṣṭhas tad annam amṛtopamam
c sādhu rāmeti saṃbhāṣya svam āśramam upāgamat
a tasmin gate mahātejā rāghavaḥ prītamānasaḥ
c saṃsmṛtya kālavākyāni tato duḥkham upeyivān
a duḥkhena ca susaṃtaptaḥ smṛtvā tad ghoradarśanam
c avānmukho dīnamanā vyāhartuṃ na śaśāka ha
a tato buddhyā viniścitya kālavākyāni rāghavaḥ
c naitad astīti coktvā sa tūṣṇīm āsīn mahāyaśāḥ
a avāṅmukham atho dīnaṃ dṛṣṭvā somam ivāplutam
c rāghavaṃ lakṣmaṇo vākyaṃ hṛṣṭo madhuram abravīt
a na saṃtāpaṃ mahābāho madarthaṃ kartum arhasi
c pūrvanirmāṇabaddhā hi kālasya gatir īdṛśī
a jahi māṃ saumya visrabdaḥ pratijñāṃ paripālaya
c hīnapratijñāḥ kākutstha prayānti narakaṃ narāḥ
a yadi prītir mahārāja yady anugrāhyatā mayi
c jahi māṃ nirviśaṅkas tvaṃ dharmaṃ vardhaya rāghava
a lakṣmaṇena tathoktas tu rāmaḥ pracalitendriyaḥ
c mantriṇaḥ samupānīya tathaiva ca purodhasaṃ
a abravīc ca yathāvṛttaṃ teṣāṃ madhye narādhipaḥ
c durvāso'bhigamaṃ caiva pratijñāṃ tāpasasya ca
a tac chrutvā mantriṇaḥ sarve sopādhyāyāḥ samāsata
c vasiṣṭhas tu mahātejā vākyam etad uvāca ha
a dṛṣṭam etan mahābāho kṣayaṃ te lomaharṣaṇam
c lakṣmaṇena viyogaś ca tava rāma mahāyaśaḥ
a tyajainaṃ balavān kālo mā pratijñāṃ vṛthā kṛthāḥ
c vinaṣṭāyāṃ pratijñāyāṃ dharmo hi vilayaṃ vrajet
a tato dharme vinaṣṭe tu trailokye sacarācaram
c sadevarṣigaṇaṃ sarvaṃ vinaśyeta na saṃśayaḥ
a sa tvaṃ puruṣaśārdūla trailokyasyābhipālanam
c lakṣmaṇasya vadhenādya jagat svasthaṃ kuruṣva ha
a teṣāṃ tat samavetānāṃ vākyaṃ dharmārthasaṃhitam
c śrutvā pariṣado madhye rāmo lakṣmaṇam abravīt
a visarjaye tvāṃ saumitre mā bhūd dharmaviparyayaḥ
c tyāgo vadho vā vihitaḥ sādhūnām ubhayaṃ samam
a rāmeṇa bhāṣite vākye bāṣpavyākulitekṣaṇaḥ
c lakṣmaṇas tvaritaḥ prāyāt svagṛhaṃ na viveśa ha
a sa gatvā sarayūtīram upaspṛśya kṛtāñjaliḥ
c nigṛhya sarvasrotāṃsi niḥśvāsaṃ na mumoca ha
a anucchvasantaṃ yuktaṃ taṃ saśakrāḥ sāpsarogaṇāḥ
c devāḥ sarṣigaṇāḥ sarve puṣpair avakiraṃs tadā
a adṛśyaṃ sarvam anujaiḥ saśarīraṃ mahābalam
c pragṛhya lakṣmaṇaṃ śakro divaṃ saṃpraviveśa ha
a tato viṣṇoś caturbhāgam āgataṃ surasattamāḥ
c hṛṣṭāḥ pramuditāḥ sarve 'pūjayan ṛṣibhiḥ saha
a visṛjya lakṣmaṇaṃ rāmo duḥkhaśokasamanvitaḥ
c purodhasaṃ mantriṇaś ca naigamāṃś cedam abravīt
a adya rājye 'bhiṣekṣyāmi bharataṃ dharmavatsalam
c ayodhyāyāṃ patiṃ vīraṃ tato yāsyāmy ahaṃ vanam
a praveśayata saṃbhārān mā bhūt kālātyayo yathā
c adyaivāhaṃ gamiṣyāmi lakṣmaṇena gatāṃ gatim
a tac chrutvā rāghaveṇoktaṃ sarvāḥ prakṛtayo bhṛśam
c mūrdhabhiḥ praṇatā bhūmau gatasattvā ivābhavan
a bharataś ca visaṃjño 'bhūc chrutvā rāmasya bhāṣitam
c rājyaṃ vigarhayām āsa rāghavaṃ cedam abravīt
a satyena hi śape rājan svargaloke na caiva hi
c na kāmaye yathā rājyaṃ tvāṃ vinā raghunandana
a imau kuśīlavau rājann abhiṣiñca narādhipa
c kosaleṣu kuśaṃ vīram uttareṣu tathā lavam
a śatrughnasya tu gacchantu dūtās tvaritavikramāḥ
c idaṃ gamanam asmākaṃ svargāyākhyāntu māciram
a tac chrutvā bharatenoktaṃ dṛṣṭvā cāpi hy adho mukhān
c paurān duḥkhena saṃtaptān vasiṣṭho vākyam abravīt
a vatsa rāma imāḥ paśya dharaṇīṃ prakṛtīr gatāḥ
c jñātvaiṣām īpsitaṃ kāryaṃ mā caiṣāṃ vipriyaṃ kṛthāḥ
a vasiṣṭhasya tu vākyena utthāpya prakṛtījanam
c kiṃ karomīti kākutsthaḥ sarvān vacanam abravīt
a tataḥ sarvāḥ prakṛtayo rāmaṃ vacanam abruvan
c gacchantam anugacchāmo yato rāma gamiṣyasi
a eṣā naḥ paramā prītir eṣa dharmaḥ paro mataḥ
c hṛdgatā naḥ sadā tuṣṭis tavānugamane dṛḍhā
a paureṣu yadi te prītir yadi sneho hy anuttamaḥ
c saputradārāḥ kākutstha samaṃ gacchāma satpatham
a tapovanaṃ vā durgaṃ vā nadīm ambhonidhiṃ tathā
c vayaṃ te yadi na tyājyāḥ sarvān no naya īśvara
a sa teṣāṃ niścayaṃ jñātvā kṛtāntaṃ ca nirīkṣyaca
c paurāṇāṃ dṛḍhabhaktiṃ ca bāḍham ity eva so 'bravīt
a evaṃ viniścayaṃ kṛtvā tasminn ahani rāghavaḥ
c kosaleṣu kuśaṃ vīram uttareṣu tathā lavam
a abhiṣiñcan mahātmānāv ubhāv eva kuśīlavau
c rathānāṃ tu sahasrāṇi trīṇi nāgāyutāni ca
a daśa cāśvasahasrāṇi ekaikasya dhanaṃ dadau
c bahuratnau bahudhanau hṛṣṭapuṣṭajanāvṛtau
a abhiṣicya tu tau vīrau prasthāpya svapure tathā
c dūtān saṃpreṣayām āsa śatrughnāya mahātmane
a te dūtā rāmavākyena coditā laghuvikramāḥ
c prajagmur madhurāṃ śīghraṃ cakrur vāsaṃ na cādhvani
a tatas tribhir aho rātraiḥ saṃprāpya madhurām atha
c śatrughnāya yathāvṛttam ācakhyuḥ sarvam eva tat
a lakṣmaṇasya parityāgaṃ pratijñāṃ rāghavasya ca
c putrayor abhiṣekaṃ ca paurānugamanaṃ tathā
a kuśasya nagarī ramyā vindhyaparvatarodhasi
c kuśāvatīti nāmnā sā kṛtā rāmeṇa dhīmatā
a śrāvitā ca purī ramyā śrāvatīti lavasya ca
c ayodhyāṃ vijanāṃ caiva bharataṃ rāghavānugam
a evaṃ sarvaṃ nivedyāśu śatrughnāya mahātmane
c viremus te tato dūtās tvara rājann iti bruvan
a śrutvā taṃ ghorasaṃkāśaṃ kulakṣayam upasthitam
c prakṛtīs tu samānīya kāñcanaṃ ca purohitam
a teṣāṃ sarvaṃ yathāvṛttam ākhyāya raghunandanaḥ
c ātmanaś ca viparyāsaṃ bhaviṣyaṃ bhrātṛbhiḥ saha
a tataḥ putradvayaṃ vīraḥ so 'bhyaṣiñcan narādhipaḥ
c subāhur madhurāṃ lebhe śatrughātī ca vaidiśam
a dvidhākṛtvā tu tāṃ senāṃ mādhurīṃ putrayor dvayoḥ
c dhanadhānyasamāyuktau sthāpayām āsa pārthivau
a tato visṛjya rājānaṃ vaidiśe śatrughātinam
c jagāma tvarito 'yodhyāṃ rathenaikena rāghavaḥ
a sa dadarśa mahātmānaṃ jvalantam iva pāvakam
c kṣaumasūkṣmāmbaradharaṃ munibhiḥ sārdham akṣayaiḥ
a so 'bhivādya tato rāmaṃ prāñjaliḥ prayatendriyaḥ
c uvāca vākyaṃ dharmajño dharmam evānucintayan
a kṛtvābhiṣekaṃ sutayor yuktaṃ rāghavayor dhanaiḥ
c tavānugamane rājan viddhi māṃ kṛtaniścayam
a na cānyad atra vaktavyaṃ dustaraṃ tava śāsanam
c tyaktuṃ nārhasi māṃ vīra bhaktimantaṃ viśeṣataḥ
a tasya tāṃ buddhim aklībāṃ vijñāya raghunandanaḥ
c bāḍham ity eva śatrughnaṃ rāmo vacanam abravīt
a tasya vākyasya vākyānte vānarāḥ kāmarūpiṇaḥ
c ṛkṣarākṣasasaṃghāś ca samāpetur anekaśaḥ
a devaputrā ṛṣisutā gandharvāṇāṃ sutās tathā
c rāma kṣayaṃ viditvā te sarva eva samāgatāḥ
a te rāmam abhivādyāhuḥ sarva eva samāgatāḥ
c tavānugamane rājan saṃprāptāḥ sma mahāyaśaḥ
a yadi rāma vināsmābhir gacches tvaṃ puruṣarṣabha
c yamadaṇḍam ivodyamya tvayā sma vinipātitāḥ
a evaṃ teṣāṃ vacaḥ śrutvā ṛṣkavānararakṣasām
c vibhīṣaṇam athovāca madhuraṃ ślakṣṇayā girā
a yāvat prajā dhariṣyanti tāvat tvaṃ vai vibhīṣaṇa
c rākṣasendra mahāvīrya laṅkāsthaḥ svaṃ dhariṣyasi
a prajāḥ saṃrakṣa dharmeṇa nottaraṃ vaktum arhasi
a tam evam uktvā kākutstho hanūmantam athābravīt
c jīvite kṛtabuddhis tvaṃ mā pratijñāṃ vilopaya
a matkathāḥ pracariṣyanti yāval loke harīśvara
c tāvat tvaṃ dhārayan prāṇān pratijñām anupālaya
a tathaivam uktvā kākutsthaḥ sarvāṃs tān ṛkṣavānarān
c mayā sārdhaṃ prayāteti tadā tān rāghavo 'bravīt
a prabhātāyāṃ tu śarvaryāṃ pṛthuvakṣā mahāyaśāḥ
c rāmaḥ kamalapatrākṣaḥ purodhasam athābravīt
a agnihotraṃ vrajatv agre sarpir jvalitapāvakam
c vājapeyātapatraṃ ca śobhayānaṃ mahāpatham
a tato vasiṣṭhas tejasvī sarvaṃ niravaśeṣataḥ
c cakāra vidhivad dharmyaṃ mahāprāsthānikaṃ vidhim
a tataḥ kṣaumāmbaradharo brahma cāvartayan param
c kuśān gṛhītvā pāṇibhyāṃ prasajya prayayāv atha
a avyāharan kva cit kiṃ cin niśceṣṭo niḥsukhaḥ pathi
c nirjagāma gṛhāt tasmād dīpyamāno yathāṃśumān
a rāmasya pārśve savye tu padmā śrīḥ susamāhitā
c dakṣiṇe hrīr viśālākṣī vyavasāyas tathāgrataḥ
a śarā nānāvidhāś cāpi dhanur āyatavigraham
c anuvrajanti kākutsthaṃ sarve puruṣavigrahāḥ
a vedā brāhmaṇarūpeṇa sāvitrī sarvarakṣiṇī
c oṃkāro 'tha vaṣaṭkāraḥ sarve rāmam anuvratāḥ
a ṛṣayaś ca mahātmānaḥ sarva eva mahīsurāḥ
c anvagacchanta kākutsthaṃ svargadvāram upāgatam
a taṃ yāntam anuyānti sma antaḥpuracarāḥ striyaḥ
c savṛddhabāladāsīkāḥ savarṣavarakiṃkarāḥ
a sāntaḥpuraś ca bharataḥ śatrughnasahito yayau
c rāmavratam upāgamya rāghavaṃ samanuvratāḥ
a tato viprā mahātmānaḥ sāgnihotrāḥ samāhitāḥ
c saputradārāḥ kākutstham anvagacchan mahāmatim
a mantriṇo bhṛtyavargāś ca saputrāḥ sahabāndhavāḥ
c sānugā rāghavaṃ sarve anvagacchan prahṛṣṭavat
a tataḥ sarvāḥ prakṛtayo hṛṣṭapuṣṭajanāvṛtāḥ
c anujagmuḥ pragacchantaṃ rāghavaṃ guṇarañjitāḥ
a snātaṃ pramuditaṃ sarvaṃ hṛṣṭapuṣpam anuttamam
c dṛptaṃ kilikilāśabdaiḥ sarvaṃ rāmam anuvratam
a na tatra kaś cid dīno 'bhūd vrīḍito vāpi duḥkhitaḥ
c hṛṣṭaṃ pramuditaṃ sarvaṃ babhūva paramādbhutam
a draṣṭukāmo 'tha niryāṇaṃ rājño jānapado janaḥ
c saṃprāptaḥ so 'pi dṛṣṭvaiva saha sarvair anuvrataḥ
a ṛkṣavānararakṣāṃsi janāś ca puravāsinaḥ
c agachan parayā bhaktyā pṛṣṭhataḥ susamāhitāḥ
a adhyardhayojanaṃ gatvā nadīṃ paścān mukhāśritām
c sarayūṃ puṇyasalilāṃ dadarśa raghunandanaḥ
a atha tasmin muhūrte tu brahmā lokapitāmahaḥ
c sarvaiḥ parivṛto devair ṛṣibhiś ca mahātmabhiḥ
a āyayau yatra kākutsthaḥ svargāya samupasthitaḥ
c vimānaśatakoṭībhir divyābhir abhisaṃvṛtaḥ
a papāta puṣpavṛṣṭiś ca vāyumuktā mahaughavat
a tasmiṃs tūryaśatākīrṇe gandharvāpsarasaṃkule
c sarayūsalilaṃ rāmaḥ padbhyāṃ samupacakrame
a tataḥ pitāmaho vāṇīm antarikṣād abhāṣata
c āgaccha viṣṇo bhadraṃ te diṣṭyā prāpto 'si rāghava
a bhrātṛbhiḥ saha devābhaiḥ praviśasva svakāṃ tanum
c vaiṣṇavīṃ tāṃ mahātejas tad ākāśaṃ sanātanam
a tvaṃ hi lokagatir deva na tvāṃ ke cit prajānate
c ṛte māyāṃ viśālākṣa tava pūrvaparigrahām
a tvam acintyaṃ mahad bhūtam akṣayaṃ sarvasaṃgraham
c yām icchasi mahātejas tāṃ tanuṃ praviśa svayam
a pitāmahavacaḥ śrutvā viniścitya mahāmatiḥ
c viveśa vaiṣṇavaṃ tejaḥ saśarīraḥ sahānujaḥ
a tato viṣṇugataṃ devaṃ pūjayanti sma devatāḥ
c sādhyā marudgaṇāś caiva sendrāḥ sāgnipurogamāḥ
a ye ca divyā ṛṣigaṇā gandharvāpsarasaś ca yāḥ
c suparṇanāgayakṣāś ca daityadānavarākṣasāḥ
a sarvaṃ hṛṣṭaṃ pramuditaṃ sarvaṃ pūrṇamanoratham
c sādhu sādhv iti tat sarvaṃ tridivaṃ gatakalmaṣam
a atha viṣṇur mahātejāḥ pitāmaham uvāca ha
c eṣāṃ lokāñ janaughānāṃ dātum arhasi suvrata
a ime hi sarve snehān mām anuyātā manasvinaḥ
c bhaktā bhājayitavyāś ca tyaktātmānaś ca matkṛte
a tac chrutvā viṣṇuvacanaṃ brahmā lokaguruḥ prabhuḥ
c lokān sāntānikān nāma yāsyantīme samāgatāḥ
a yac ca tiryaggataṃ kiṃ cid rāmam evānucintayat
c prāṇāṃs tyakṣyati bhaktyā vai saṃtāne tu nivatsyati
e sarvair eva guṇair yukte brahmalokād anantare
a vānarāś ca svakāṃ yonim ṛkṣāś caiva tathā yayuḥ
c yebhyo viniḥsṛtā ye ye surādibhyaḥ susaṃbhavāḥ
a ṛṣibhyo nāgayakṣebhyas tāṃs tān eva prapedire
c tathoktavati deveśe gopratāram upāgatāḥ
a bhejire sarayūṃ sarve harṣapūrṇāśruviklavāḥ
c avagāhya jalaṃ yo yaḥ prāṇī hy āsīt prahṛṣṭavat
a mānuṣaṃ deham utsṛjya vimānaṃ so 'dhyarohata
c tiryagyonigatāś cāpi saṃprāptāḥ sarayūjalam
a divyā divyena vapuṣā devā dīptā ivābhavan
c gatvā tu sarayūtoyaṃ sthāvarāṇi carāṇi ca
a prāpya tat toyavikledaṃ devalokam upāgaman
c devānāṃ yasya yā yonir vānarā ṛṣka rākṣasāḥ
a tām eva viviśuḥ sarve devān nikṣipya cāmbhasi
c tathā svargagataṃ sarvaṃ kṛtvā lokagurur divam
a jagāma tridaśaiḥ sārdhaṃ hṛṣṭair hṛṣṭo mahāmatiḥ
